  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_53180b21-050f-4d9f-8e4d-04679d1dc665'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer16623323465181358179">Xcor, leader of the Band of Bastards, convicted of treason against the Blind King, is facing a brutal interrogation and torturous death at the hands of the Black Dagger Brotherhood. Yet after a life marked by cruelty and evil deeds, he accepts his soldier’s fate, his sole regret the loss of a sacred female who was never his: the Chosen Layla.<br/> <br/>Layla alone knows the truth th</span>
  <span id="freeText16623323465181358179" style="display:none">Xcor, leader of the Band of Bastards, convicted of treason against the Blind King, is facing a brutal interrogation and torturous death at the hands of the Black Dagger Brotherhood. Yet after a life marked by cruelty and evil deeds, he accepts his soldier’s fate, his sole regret the loss of a sacred female who was never his: the Chosen Layla.<br /> <br />Layla alone knows the truth that will save Xcor’s life. But revealing his sacrifice and his hidden heritage will expose them both and destroy everything Layla holds dear—even her role of mother to her precious young. Torn between love and loyalty, she must summon the courage to stand up against the only family she has for the only man she will ever love. Yet even if Xcor is somehow granted a reprieve, he and Layla would have to confront a graver challenge: bridging the chasm that divides their worlds without paving the way for a future of even greater war, desolation, and death.<br /> <br />As a dangerous old enemy returns to Caldwell, and the identity of a new deity is revealed, nothing is certain or safe in the world of the Black Dagger Brotherhood, not even true love... or destinies that have long seemed set in stone.</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1606479670" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9948667325559310970"><b>What in the fresh hell is this flaming pile of poo???</b><br/><br/>(psssst...obligatory ***<b>Spoilers Ahead!!!</b>*** tag. Turn back now if you don't want to be spoiled!)<br/><br/>I am having trouble even trying to process what just happened here. HOW could Ward have screwed up this story so badly? I didn't think it was possible to drop the ball and have it roll so far under the damn couch. By writing this review I'm over here sticking my arm underneath the furniture, cringing at the dust bunnies that I'm touching while retr</span>
  <span id="freeText9948667325559310970" style="display:none"><b>What in the fresh hell is this flaming pile of poo???</b><br /><br />(psssst...obligatory ***<b>Spoilers Ahead!!!</b>*** tag. Turn back now if you don't want to be spoiled!)<br /><br />I am having trouble even trying to process what just happened here. HOW could Ward have screwed up this story so badly? I didn't think it was possible to drop the ball and have it roll so far under the damn couch. By writing this review I'm over here sticking my arm underneath the furniture, cringing at the dust bunnies that I'm touching while retrieving Ward's ball. In case you can't figure out the symbolism, the dust bunnies are the random WTF? moments in this story that I'm going to have to talk about. <br /><br />I came out of review-writing sabbatical FOR THIS CRAP?<br /><br />How is it even possible for me to have to 1 star a book in one of my most-beloved series of all time? I mean, sure, the BDB has had cringe-worthy and frustrating moments before, but <i>not on this scale</i>.<br /><br /><b>EVERY SINGLE plot direction went awry in this book.</b> Every. Single. One. <br /><br />Let's dig in, shall we?<br /><br /><b>1. Qhuinn finally done lost it.</b> You know, I never fully jumped on the 'Q's an a-hole' train before now. I kind of felt like people went in too hard on him in the past. He had a whole lot of hell to deal with in his life, and no one to teach him how to get past it. Blay, on the other hand, had the nurturing and loving that was necessary to shape him into a decent <s>human being</s> vampire. But all of that went out the window when HE PULLED A MOTHEREFFING GUN on the mother of his child and SHOT UP A ROOM that his children were in. <br /><br />And Layla was the one who needed to exit? If I were Wrath, both of their asses would have been tossed out on the street (and I sympathized with Layla in this situation). <br /><br />I didn't even care about the Blay drama (which was completely unnecessary when there was Layla drama going on...too many open plots going, imo. Q and B should have worked out their lingering baggage in a previous or future book.). Yeah, so Q went off and said something he didn't mean to Blay. Big deal. Who hasn't done that? Are we just going to ignore that the meathead shot a damn gun in the house??? Layla should have been spitting angry. Yes, like a lizard or a dragon or whatever real or imagined creature spits. <br /><br />And the fact that NO ONE is trying to put Q in therapy is a head scratcher. He has REAL issues that need to be dealt with.<br /><br />*Edit* Also need to add that Qhuinn denying his own daughter affection and care because she looked like her mom is all kinds of wrong and f*cked up. <br /><br /><b>2. Wrath shuts down Xcor's execution.</b> To be fair, I think that Wrath was the only one who would have been able to shut it down. But how was Wrath able to 'get over it' so quickly? Yes, Wrath can smell the truth, but if I was him, I would have wanted to know more, or I would have at least made Xcor jump through a few more hoops before giving him full access to conjugal visits with Layla in a BDB-owned property. Was this lazy writing on the author's part to move the story along so she had time to fit eleventybillion other plot finishers into one book? Did it occur to her that she could have wrapped up X and L's story while still leaving loose ends with Xcor and the others? More on this later when we get to Tohr's role in this debacle.<br /><br /><b>3. Layla and Xcor finally get it on in the most boring climax (no pun intended) ever.</b> Layla <i>finally</i> quits dancing around her feelings in front of the brothers and you'd think that she'd have to fight hard to get epic alone time (maybe sex in a forbidden place while on the run). But nope. Wrath gives the go-ahead nod, and the injured walk to the bedroom for some loving and underdeveloped sex. Yawn. THIS was what we've been waiting for? <br /><br />And why did Layla wait so long to spill the beans about Tohr? Why not say something when Xcor was ABOUT TO BE KILLED??? Maybe that would have given V or Tohr at least a moment's pause? WTF woman? <br /><br />Also, I found it weird that X and L didn't end up discussing the kids until further in the book. Oh, btw, I had the twins honey. <br /><br /><b>4. Trez and Selena redux.</b> Too Soon. Too Soon. This shouldn't have come up for at least another 5 books down the road. I would've rather had a peek at Marhkus instead. Trez should be living and trying to cope for a while, while we see him spending time drawing close to iAm and his sister in law (I would've liked to have seen a Catra cameo) and working on that family unit. <br /><br />*Edit* I realize that Selena is tied to Lassiter stepping into his new role, so I get what happened to a point. I just wish that Lassiter had been able to find something else to dig in to, instead of this <i>right now</i>.<br /><br />...and again with the 'little to no questions' angle. Okay, so he might not be wanting to look a pain-reducing gift-horse in the mouth, but why aren't we seeing at least a slight bit of the brain swirl that <u>must</u> be happening to him? He vaguely understands that Therese is 'different' from Selena (although not so different, when we as the reader know that she is a reincarnation), but 'new girl' really only <i>looks</i> like his Chosen. Her personality seems drastically different. And I guess this is good for moving on? *shrug* But he takes to Therese like a duck to water.<br /><br />She's familiar. She's different. She's familiar. She's different. My mind would be working overtime. Trez just gets a migraine. Cool, I guess... <br /><br /><b>5. Tohr Part 1.</b> Tohr also done lost his mind. What was that garbage with Layla? The BDB have never been the most forward-thinking feminists, but they've always at least been <i>somewhat</i> respectful to the women. Most of their borderline sexism comes from off-color (generally meant to be lighthearted) comments and 'guy talk'...not from going toe-to-toe with the ladies. This scene had me feeling all kinds of uncomfortable. It didn't ring authentic to Tohr, even if he was due to snap. I would have preferred a long, drag-out, knock-down scene with Wrath (or Xcor) to this mess.<br /><br /><b>6. Tohr Part 2.</b> AT BEST, Tohr and X could have had a tentative handshake (even that would have been pushing it...a head nod would have worked for me) and an understanding that they would come back to their feelings later. AT BEST. This 'happy little bow' garbage was rushed and wrong for this book.<br /><br /><b>7. Tohr Part 3.</b> I'm not telling him to get over Wellsie, but...he's being unfair to Autumn. She STILL reads as a begrudging number 2 by an extra-long-overextended mile. In retrospect, his story would have worked better had he returned to the Brotherhood as a single man and gone at least a few more years (Lord knows we'll still be reading this series then...we still haven't seen Phury's predicted baby or Murhder's return) before finding Autumn. Maybe then, he wouldn't have been dealing with such fresh wounds that weren't even close to being ready to heal. FFS, poor Autumn has the patience of a saint. She doesn't deserve being Tohr's sex toy who he happens to also care about, but not deeply love as much as he should.<br /><br /><b>8. V and Jane - again.</b> Sigh. I don't even know what to say here. This is not the first or even second go-round with these two. We're spoon-fed lies about how this couple functions differently than other couples, but are still (supposedly) very much functioning. But they're not, as witnessed in this book (which contradicts the last awkward no-baby-let's-fistbump conversation). And I don't care. V wants to cheat. I don't care. V feels distant from Jane. I don't care. I really hope that all of this is at least leading up to a scene where we finally see something worthwhile from these two. An epic reunion (and finally putting this mess to bed) is in order.<br /><br /><b>9. Throe gets creepy and the lore goes wonky.</b> So we have extra magic now? Did I miss Throe's tie to the Omega, or was new world magic just plopped into the story that didn't exist before? I thought Lash was coming back? I'm so confused. <br /><br />*Edit * I found out after reading a Ward fan gathering Q &amp; A that Throe's book/shadow situation is tied to Davina (from the Fallen Angels series, another Ward offering) trying to break free, and that Lash will be back, and that there will be some changes coming for The Omega, so I guess there is a reason for all of this nonsense, even if it was introduced in a weird way that I don't like. <br /><br />And I don't understand why Throe had a respectable, almost redeemable moment in the Fallen Angels series if he was just gonna end up this far gone. I wish that dark savior moment of his had never happened because it still messes with my head. I keep thinking that Throe's villain turn might be temporary, but nah...I guess we're going full V. And that's fine. The series needs villains. I just wish that we hadn't seen brief snippets of Throe as a potential ally for good in the past. <br /><br /><b>10. The ending - a.k.a. The Brady Bunch ain't got nothing on these brothers.</b> There was NO reason the BoB needed to move into the mansion. None. With all of the property that the BDB owns? They couldn't have been given their own barracks/dorm/apartment complex/office building/old ranch, hospital, amusement park, whatever? Yes, they're all gonna fight together now *wonder <s>twins</s> brother powers activate!* Yippee! (?) But in the same damn house? So we're just trusting them with the kids now after one fight? Again, we as the readers know that the BoB aren't all bad, but the Brothers aren't privy to the info that we get.<br /><br />Come.<br />On. <br />Now.<br /><br />I thought I recoiled when Rhage called Ruhn son. Boy, was I only getting warmed up for the main event. Ward went full summer camp with this BS. Xcor and Qhuinn bonding? Q letting X hold the babies? We couldn't have had this happen S-L-O-W-L-Y over the course of a few books? In THIS book, we might have seen Q being okay with X and Layla being together, but not ready for the kids to get up close and personal just yet. And that would've been more organic. X could have been patient and been happy just to have his girl for now. He could have bonded with the kids in the future. <br /><br />As well...<br />Not everyone has to be related.<br />Not everyone has to work together.<br />Not everyone has to live together.<br /><br />Sometimes people can just be respectful acquaintences, or buddies on the 'let's grab a beer on Friday' level. They don't all have to love and hug and share Christmas together. <br /><br />What's next? Are the rest of the Shadows and some Sympaths going to join the fray? And by 'join', I mean hang out in the world's largest billiards room? Perhaps the dining hall could be expanded to a cafeteria. <br /><br />Fritz must have one hell of a staff to clean up after these people who can't seem to do it for themselves...ever.<br /><br />I feel like I might have more to say after I'm able to process more, but this is what I've got for now.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9948667325559310970" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1618017766" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1618017766" />
    <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish"><img alt="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398981306p2/1113032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1618017766?book_show_action=true">Apr 22, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=format-kindle-or-kindle-compatible">format-kindle-or-kindle-compatible</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=not-enough-romance">not-enough-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=series-black-dagger-brotherhood-war">series-black-dagger-brotherhood-war</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=own-have-read">own-have-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=author-jr-ward-jessica-bird">author-jr-ward-jessica-bird</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1618017766" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17150116714783225780"><b>Full <i>rant</i>view now posted</b><br/><br/>I'm am very conflicted in regards to this installment of the <i>Black Dagger Brotherhood</i> series. There were a couple things I enjoyed, but those things got lost in the bigger picture. <br/><br/>It's taken me days to process it all and try to decide how best to write this review. I've decided to break it down into sections, with spoilers hidden.<br/><br/>I'll start with Xcor and Layla because this is their story, and it was a long time coming.<br/><br/><b>Xcor and Layla (no spoilers) - </b> I have always liked L</span>
  <span id="freeText17150116714783225780" style="display:none"><b>Full <i>rant</i>view now posted</b><br /><br />I'm am very conflicted in regards to this installment of the <i>Black Dagger Brotherhood</i> series. There were a couple things I enjoyed, but those things got lost in the bigger picture. <br /><br />It's taken me days to process it all and try to decide how best to write this review. I've decided to break it down into sections, with spoilers hidden.<br /><br />I'll start with Xcor and Layla because this is their story, and it was a long time coming.<br /><br /><b>Xcor and Layla (no spoilers) - </b> I have always liked Layla because I see her as a product of crappy parenting. Her upbringing sucked, being raised to serve, her worth being found in and determined by her service to others. Her existence was serving the Brotherhood which meant not having a chance to think for herself, to dream, to hope for more - or to realize that there even<i>could</i> be more. I was thrilled when the Chosen were set free of their prison and allowed to live free, at last.<br /><br />From his first appearance in the series, I loved Xcor and was excited to see where his story would go. No doubt he was a complete douche waffle bastard in the beginning, but I saw him as a male in need of redemption, and couldn't wait to see that redemption unfold. I wasn't disappointed. In fact, I love him and his back story even more! <br /><br /> I am thrilled beyond thrilled that Xcor and Layla finally have their <i>happily ever after.</i> It wasn't easy - but the most beautiful romances seldom are. They had many seemingly insurmountable obstacles, but they overcame them. They are the perfect example of opposites attracting, and I am glad this was their story. It was time. <br /><br /><b>Qhuinn (and Blay) - </b> Qhuinn is okay. He's never been one of my favorite characters, but I did enjoy his book and wanted him to get his HEA. But I have to say - he's an ass in this story. I get why he freaks out, but <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[pulling a gun in the same room with his young? Pointing it at his mate? Calling the <i>mahmen</i> of his young a whore and all the other horrible things he said to her... and to Blay. Then he doesn't get why Blay leaves him? He doesn't understand why Blay is broken at being told to butt out, that he's not the father of their kids, when so far all we've heard is that they are, the three of them, equally the parents of Rhamp and Lyric. And then he has the nerve to expect Blay to just get over it like it wasn't a big deal. No. Not okay. He's dead to me. He can just walk his sorry fanny into the Fade for all I care. Blay and Layla can parent alone and the young will be better for it.<br /><br />Also, when Blay and Qhuinn finally do makeup it was too fast. Qhuinn did a wonderful thing making Blay the full father, legally, but there was no groveling, no sincere apologies, nothing that tells me Qhuinn had any real remorse, and I needed that more than I needed a piece of paper - a paper that should have been the least of the repercussions of his behavior. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>V (and Jane)</b> - What the hell happened here? Why are we even doing this? First off, they had their story a long time ago, then it was revisited with marital discord in a book within the last few years. Now here we are again being subjected to this couple <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ with V contemplating an affair? Seriously? Forget the morality issue of cheating. This is the BDB world where mates would never dream of straying or hurting one another, so why is this happening? Do you know? 'Cuz I sure as hell do not.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Why can't the WARDen just leave V alone?! She doesn't like him and he doesn't like her. Is she intentionally torturing him, or did someone spike her Rice Krispies?<br /><br /><i>What. ever! </i><br /><br /><b>Trez (and Selena) - </b> Okay, here's another giant WTF??? It wasn't bad enough that Ward betrayed her readers (and the romance genre) by killing Selena off in that hot mess called <i>The Shadows</i>? What is happening to this series?? These vampires' lives are filled with drama, must there be so much <i>unnecessary</i> drama thrown in? NONE of this had to happen!! The BDB is beginning to read like a soap opera, for Fade's sake! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ In her Cincinnati Chosen Book Signing, the WARDen says that Selena had to die so that Lassiter, as the new Scribe Virgin, could do something big by bringing her back.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Maybe someday down the road it will make sense to me, but for now it just sounds like more backpedaling and a long, contrived stretch at trying to rectify a horrible wrong.<br /><br /><b>Tohr (and his role) - </b> I'm at a loss here. I'm embarrassed on his behalf for the crappy story he was given in this book. Some things I get, some I wanted to scream at! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ So, I am 100% behind Tohr and Qhuinn going behind Wrath's back to hunt Xcor. I get it. I expect it. I support it as part of the story. It's Tohr's job to protect the King, and Xcor DID put a bullet in Wrath's throat. If I was Tohr, I'd go against the King's wishes and hunt the head Bastard too. I would and I would expect Tohr to do the same. The hatred between Tohr and Xcor is and always has been real. But their "Tohr, he's your brother" insta-forgiveness makes no sense! Too fast. Too shallow. Sooooo NOT Tohr.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> And I understand a lot of this was taking place on the night of what would have been Wellsie's birthday so Tohr's an emotional wreck, but for gawd's sake, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Autumn is too damned understanding! I wouldn't expect jealousy from her, but I WOULD expect a little more loyalty and sensitivity from Tohr. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br />Like I said, his role in <i>The Chosen</i> is an embarrassment, not only to himself but to the Brotherhood he defends and to us, the readers.<br /><br /><b>Lassiter - </b> Sweet Virgin on a pogo stick! This is going to be one wild ride!<br /><br /><b>The bottom line - </b> There was so much potential to <i>The Chosen</i> that, sadly, wasn't given the time needed to develop. It could've been beautiful but instead it was hurried. It could have been poignant but instead it was shallow. <br /><br />Since 2008 when I read my first <i>Black Dagger Brotherhood</i> story I have been a die-hard, fiercely loyal fan. When things started getting a bit wonky... say, about the time of Phury's almost non-existent <i>happily ever after</i>, I still stood tall and proud and defended everything the WARDen gave us. It breaks my heart to tell you that I no longer feel that admiration for and devotion to her and her stories. <br /><br />We pay a premium price for these books and we shouldn't have to wade through what amounts to nothing more than filler in the form of contrived drama, just to get to the main story line. We read romance for the <i>happily ever after</i>, as in, <i>EVER</i> after. Not 'happily 'til an author's breakfast cereal decrees otherwise.' That's not the foundation this series was built on! That's not what we longtime, die-hard, fiercely loyal fans hunger for. And saddest of all - that's not the <i>Black Dagger Brotherhood</i> I fell in love with all those years ago. <br /><br />And oh, how I miss them.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17150116714783225780" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1605555126" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1605555126?book_show_action=true">Apr 09, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1605555126" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15687405297416335895"><b>5 Stars!!!!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%2010/A9960FAD-347C-4948-B1B6-EA326A4D6FAD_zpsblhsquzx.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492089137i/22481076._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo A9960FAD-347C-4948-B1B6-EA326A4D6FAD_zpsblhsquzx.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>The Chosen</i> is the book all BDB fans have been waiting for for years! I know I have. I had such high hopes for this book and was a little nervous to start it, but I can say with absolute certainly, it did not disappoint! In fact, it’s for sure in my top 5 BDB books. I loved it so much! <br/><br/>  Ever since Xcor came on the scene, I was intrigued by him. I know he wasn’t a ‘good guy’ at first, but with time and love, he changed. His and Layla’s story was complicated and honestly, I wasn’t</span>
  <span id="freeText15687405297416335895" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars!!!!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%2010/A9960FAD-347C-4948-B1B6-EA326A4D6FAD_zpsblhsquzx.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492089137i/22481076._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo A9960FAD-347C-4948-B1B6-EA326A4D6FAD_zpsblhsquzx.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>The Chosen</i> is the book all BDB fans have been waiting for for years! I know I have. I had such high hopes for this book and was a little nervous to start it, but I can say with absolute certainly, it did not disappoint! In fact, it’s for sure in my top 5 BDB books. I loved it so much! <br><br>  Ever since Xcor came on the scene, I was intrigued by him. I know he wasn’t a ‘good guy’ at first, but with time and love, he changed. His and Layla’s story was complicated and honestly, I wasn’t sure if or how they could have a happily ever after, but I felt they deserved it more than most.<br><br><i>The Chosen</i> centers around Layla and Xcor, and you also got a lot of Xcor’s background you didn’t have before. My heart broke for these two. It felt like they were fighting a losing battle at times, but they loved each other so truly. Layla doesn’t care about Xcor’s past or his deformed face/body, she only cares about who he is now and how he treats her. She loves him. He loves her. But will their love be enough?<br><br>  Of course this story wasn’t only Layla and Xcor’s. There were many other characters that played a big part. Qhuinn and Blay, Vishous, Wrath, Thor, Lassiter, iAm and Trez. Anyone who knows me, knows I love Vishous and Qhuinn so much! They are by far my favorite 2 brothers… but my boys pissed me off in this book. Especially Qhuinn. I won’t go into it, but if you read the book- you’ll get it. I forgave him at the end, but Grrrrrrr. And I don’t even know where the V story line is going after this… I’m nervous about it though! <br><br>What I really did love was the Thor part of the book. Not at first maybe, but towards the end- Gah! Tears! I also am curious to see where Trez’s story goes. God knows he deserves some happiness. And then Lassiter. I love this! Lassiter needs his own book ASAP! It’s been announced that the next book in the BDB will be Assail’s and Sola’s. Even though they were hardly in this one, I’m looking forward to it! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%2010/77a8ad4150de1dfc786e29e92565f9f4_zpsbnabe56p.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491694729i/22437577.jpg" alt=" photo 77a8ad4150de1dfc786e29e92565f9f4_zpsbnabe56p.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9402921647272528100"><b>4 Love is a matter between souls Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/tumblr_nz6dk9zM2y1ubjp92o1_250_zps7vksozks.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><i>
  <b> **Warning There will be SPOILERS all over this bitch**** <b></b></b>
</i><br/><br/><i>***And a few long winded Rants!***</i><br/><br/><b>“Love is a matter between souls,” she said as she put her hand on the center of his chest. “Our love is between my soul and yours. Nothing is going to change that, not your past, our present … or whatever futures we may find apart. At least not on my side.”-Layla</b><br/><br/>OMG I waited so long for Xcor and Layla's love story soooo long. When I seen their book was next I </span>
  <span id="freeText9402921647272528100" style="display:none"><b>4 Love is a matter between souls Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/tumblr_nz6dk9zM2y1ubjp92o1_250_zps7vksozks.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492980074ra/22573202.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_nz6dk9zM2y1ubjp92o1_250_zps7vksozks.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>
  <b> **Warning There will be SPOILERS all over this bitch**** <b></b></b>
</i><br><br><i>***And a few long winded Rants!***</i><br><br><b>“Love is a matter between souls,” she said as she put her hand on the center of his chest. “Our love is between my soul and yours. Nothing is going to change that, not your past, our present … or whatever futures we may find apart. At least not on my side.”-Layla</b><br><br>OMG I waited so long for Xcor and Layla's love story soooo long. When I seen their book was next I was so excited I was jumping up and down and dancing like a mad woman. True story!<br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/18737415_zps8avqjhas.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492980074ra/22573200.gif" alt=" photo 18737415_zps8avqjhas.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>To get ready for The Chosen I did a reread of the whole series to have all the details fresh in my mind. Especially the Xcor and Layla details as their love story's foundation was laid out in past books. So of course I was still in the middle of my reread when The Chosen came out on the 4th. Now I'm a total spoiler whore so the first thing I did was stalk Goodreads and read every detailed review I could find. So I was not going into this read blind. I knew that Qhuinn and Tohr acted like asshats. I just didn't know how much. So it pains me to give this book anything but a 5 star review, but I have to take a star off for the jackass that is Qhuinn. I will touch more on that later. There was so much going on in this book that I'm gonna break this review up into sections and touch a little on each subject. <br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/21634951_zpsqfh1cqut.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492980073ra/22573198.gif" alt=" photo 21634951_zpsqfh1cqut.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“I love Layla. And I never once claimed her body—nor shall I. I will never seek her out nor set mine eyes upon her again. You want me to die? Well, I have. For every night she lives with you and your young, I am being murdered for I am not in her presence. So your goal is well-served and accomplished.”-Xcor</b><br><br><i> *Xcor &amp; Layla*</i><br><br>OMG Xcor and Layla were perfect! Everything I wanted and more. Xcor was sweet, sexy, and brave. His past was so sad. I totally understand why he acted the way he did. I wanted so badly to go through the pages of this book and bitch slap his mom, dad, and nursemaid. The things Xcor would say to Layla would melt my heart. Layla really shined in this book. She kicked major ass. She was standing up for her babies and her man and she wasn't backing down to no one. She was amazing, strong and so fierce. The way Layla loved Xcor was beautiful. She didn't care about his past, or his lip. All she seen was the strong, honorable warrior he was. Xcor and Layla together were amazing. There was so much romance, sweet words of love, a deep connection and tons of passion. I loved every single moment I got with these two and wished I had more. <br><br><b>“With all of my black and withered heart, I love you, my female. I deserve not the earth beneath your feet, nor the scent of you in my nose, and never the gift of your blood, but I … I am e’er grateful for the change that you wrought upon me. You have saved me, and the only thing greater than my love for you is my gratitude.”-Xcor</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/The%20Chosen_zpsjrnl660z.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492980074i/22573203._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo The Chosen_zpsjrnl660z.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“I’m not afraid of you. I’m not afraid of anything.” She lifted her chin. “When it comes to protecting the lives of my young and the male I love, I will lay my life down in the path of their destiny, and if you beat me to death because of it, I will rise from the dead and haunt you to the point of insanity. There is nothing you can do to me that will make me back down. Nothing.”-Layla</b><br><br><i>*Qhuinn &amp; Blay*</i><br><br>WTF was going on with Qhuinn. I have always felt Qhuinn was a bit of a drama queen, but damn he's done went and lost his fucking mind in this book. I would have completely understood him being mad or upset about Layla being around Xcor when she was pregnant because he didn't know that Xcor would never hurt her but Qhuinn was out of fucking control. The things he said and did. OMG! I can't even properly convey how badly he lost his shit so I will use some quotes.<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <b>“Did you go see him while you were carrying my young? Did you willingly and knowingly consort with the enemy while my fucking young were in your body?” Before she could answer him, he held up his forefinger. “And you need to think really long and hard about your answer. There is no going back from it, and it better be the truth. If I find out you lied to me, I’m going to kill you.”-Qhuinn and Layla<br>********************************************************<br>“Cut the praying! There is no one up there anymore!” He was losing it. Totally fucking losing it—“And what the hell are you asking for forgiveness for! You knowingly and willingly put my young at risk because you wanted—” He recoiled. “Jesus Christ, did you have sex with him? Did you fuck him with my children in you?” “No! I’ve never been with him like that!” “Liar,” he hollered. “You’re a lying whore—”-Qhuinn and Layla<br>*******************************************************<br>“You’re saying you never so much as kissed him.” When she didn’t answer him, he laughed harshly. “Don’t bother denying it. I can see it in your face. And you’re right, I didn’t want you, I’ve never wanted you—and don’t get it twisted. I’m not jealous, I’m fucking disgusted. I’m in love with a male of worth and I had to be with you because I needed an incubator for my son and my daughter. That and the fact you threw yourself at me in your needing was the only reason I was ever with you.”-Qhuinn<br>******************************************************<br>“Because you’re not going to mother my young anymore. You’re out of a job.” She recoiled with indignation. “What say you? I am their mahmen. I—” “Not anymore you’re not.” There was a heartbeat of silence, and then her voice exploded from her. “You can’t—you can’t take Lyric and Rhamp … you can’t take them away from me! I’m their mahmen! I have rights—” “No, you don’t. You have consorted with the enemy. You have committed treason. And you are going to be lucky to come out of this alive—not that I give a damn whether you live or die. The only thing I care about is that you never see those young again—”-Qhuinn and Layla<br>*****************************************************</b> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>Qhuinn should be the one to lose his kids and be kicked out. He was unhinged and abusive to Layla and Blay. He pulled a gun on the mother of his children while she was holding said young and he pulled a gun on his beloved mate Blay. Then he shot the gun in the house filled with not only his twins but other children and the King. He also tried to kill Xcor twice behind the king's back. He also ignored his daughter because she looked like her mom. Not wanting to touch her or even look at her. I don't know if I will ever be able to forgive Qhuinn for the way he acted in this book. And his "sorry" at the end pfff he can shove it up his ass for all I care. Blay made him do it. He didn't really mean it. He just wanted Blay back. I wanted to throat punch Qhuinn almost the whole read!<br><br><b>“Not in my fucking house!” He was so loud that the painting next to him vibrated on the plaster wall. “This is not happening in my fucking house! My shellan and my son are here—there are young under this roof. There are young in this fucking room!”-Wrath</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/dfjha_zpsbbmz4zzn.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492980367ra/22573222.gif" alt=" photo dfjha_zpsbbmz4zzn.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“Just so you and I are clear, I will never be able to get what you just said out of my head. And the same goes for the sight of you with that gun in your hand.” -Blay</b><br><br><i> *V &amp; Jane*</i><br><br>I am trying to be open minding with V and Jane. I really am, but V is starting to really piss me off. I mean did we not just play this game in Lover Unleashed when V was feeling like he missed his old Dom life and Jane and Butch thought he might cheat on her. Now here we are again and V is pulling away from Jane and thinking of cheating on his mate. He just seems so unloyal to his shellan at the drop of a hat. Every time things get rough he is ready to cheat. Grow the fuck up V. Marriage is hard especially if you are married to someone who works hard hours like say a Doctor. You feel like you don't spend enough time together then go find Jane and spend some fucking time with her. Not that Jane is off the hook. They both need to make time for their relationship. But I swear if V cheats I don't think I will be able to get over that. Just sayin'!<br><br><b>When you were contemplating cheating on your mate, it was not easy on the conscience. And not something you wanted to do in the home you shared with her.-V</b><br><br><i>* Tohr*</i><br><br>Tohr is also starting to piss me off. I loved Wellsie and I was brokenhearted when She was killed but he is remated and I feel like he is being really unfair to Autumn. She feels like second place and I don't like it. If he wasn't ready to move on then he shouldn't have. Also the way he talked to Layla was bullshit. WTF is it shit on Layla week. I was glad that he pulled his shit together at the end and I thought it was sweet what went down with Tohr and Xcor!<br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/tumblr_lk5iaizubJ1qcrzkko1_500_zps2kedhyhb.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492980073ra/22573199.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lk5iaizubJ1qcrzkko1_500_zps2kedhyhb.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> “You haven’t looked at her all night. You won’t touch her. What the hell is going on?” Shaking his head, Qhuinn said, “I’m sorry, I’m not following—” Blay jabbed his finger at the carriers. “Lyric.” “I don’t know what you’re talking about.” “Bullshit.” As Blay glared at him, Qhuinn felt his exhaustion return tenfold. “Look, I’m not—” “I know I’m not her parent, but—” “Oh, God, not that again.” He let his head fall back on his spine and stared at the paneled ceiling. “Please, not again—” “—I’m not going to stand here and let you ignore her just because she looks like Layla and you can’t stand the Chosen. I’m not going to have it, Qhuinn. It’s not fair to your daughter.”-Blay and Qhuinn</b><br><br><i> Trez &amp; Therese</i><br><br>It's too damn soon. It's been a few months and Trez already kissed Therese. I don't know how J.R. Ward is going to play this. Either Therese is a Selena look alike or Selena reincarnated. If she is a look alike then it will be like Trez is using her for her looks and I will hate that. If she is Selena, unless Lassiter tells Trez it will still fill like he is using her because she looks like his dead shellan. IDK but I'm going to try to keep an open mind. <br><br><i> Lassiter, Assail, Throe and everything else</i><br><br>Lassiter was awesome in this book, but really when is he not awesome? I love that he is the new Scribe Virgin. I can't wait to see how he runs things lol. Assail was making me sad in this book. He wasn't really in this book just talked about. He went into rehab last book and has lost his mind during detox. Now they don't know if he will pull out. Obviously Sola needs to come save him! What the FUCK is going on with Throe????? Did he just get possessed by a demon or something? All I know was he was freaking me the fuck out. For real he was creepy as hell and very evil. Watch out Brothers evil is coming. I loved Wrath, and all the Shellans in this book. They stood by Layla and supported her when Qhuinn was losing it. I am also looking forward to more about the Band of Bastards. And can I say that little Rhampage was so fucking cute. The way he kept eyeballing everyone like a little badass. Overall I really did love this book. I know with my huge rant about Qhuinn it may seem like I didn't but even though Qhuinn was a dick face Layla and Xcor were so epic they out shined his assholelyness. Lol is that a word?? Great read and I'm looking forward to the next book. J.R. Ward is amazing more than 15 books into this world(counting BDL series) and it's still exciting and fresh!<br><br><b>“Wherever I go, you shall ne’er be far from me. Wherever I sleep, you shall be beside me. What I eat, I shall share with you, and when I dream, we shall be together once again. My love, you are not gone from me ever, and I shall not take another. Till the very night I die.”-Xcor</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="9402921647272528100" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1679434256" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1679434256" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1679434256?book_show_action=true">Jun 25, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=1paranormal-lovestories">1paranormal-lovestories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=fangywarriorteams">fangywarriorteams</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1679434256" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10933063791736713174"><b>Xcor and Layla</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’m not going to apologize for who I love. In fact, I’m grateful this destiny is mine. If I had fallen for another, I wouldn’t have been forced to be this strong – and there is nothing wrong in this world or the next in finding out your own power.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>After I finished "The Chosen", the initial thought that crossed my mind was this one:<br/><br/><b>This is clearly NOT a book about the Chosen, is it?</b><br/><br/>More precisely, this is a book that talks about everyone else except about the Chosen, La</span>
  <span id="freeText10933063791736713174" style="display:none"><b>Xcor and Layla</b><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’m not going to apologize for who I love. In fact, I’m grateful this destiny is mine. If I had fallen for another, I wouldn’t have been forced to be this strong – and there is nothing wrong in this world or the next in finding out your own power.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />After I finished "The Chosen", the initial thought that crossed my mind was this one:<br /><br /><b>This is clearly NOT a book about the Chosen, is it?</b><br /><br />More precisely, this is a book that talks about everyone else except about the Chosen, Layla.<br />Because Layla in fact knew what she wants and needs for a few books now. She wants Xcor and she wants her children. <br /><br />**spoilers**<br /><br />Layla and Xcor are already in love when the book starts. They will not deny it. They will not stumble on their decisions. They will not be sorry about them. They will not ask forgiveness from the others. They are ready to die for each other. <br />In fact they could have been already dead. Nothing matters for them anymore.<br /><br /><b>This is clearly a book about the Brothers, their mates, their friends, Lassiter, the Band of Bastards. And about the READERS. Isn’t it?</b><br /><br />It is a book that talks about how all these individuals perceive the implications of the relationship between Layla and Xcor. How they feel about it, when they learn the news. How they finally accept it.<br /><br />It talks about their negative feelings, their remorse about what Layla had done. About her treachery. About the fact that she slept with the enemy. About the fact that she endangered her unborn children.<br /><br />Layla just basically waits in the whole book. She is just waiting for the others to come into terms with her actions. And this is what she gets.<br /><br />Of course Xcor and Layla will live in their love bubble for us to watch. They will finally have sex. They will finally exchange words of love, faith and commitment. But they could just as easy not say anything. <br />Because THEY KNOW. THEY FEEL.<br />The words and their sacrifices are only to convince the others. The outsiders. Even us the readers. Because as I said before, they are already where they want to be. And they absolutely know what they want.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Layla should still be able to see those kids on the regular. They need their mahmen, and whether you like it or not, she should be in their lives.”<br />“What are you saying, that she and Xcor take them to McDonald’s for fucking fries and a Coke?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />Well, apparently yes. That is exactly what Layla wants.<br /><br />Unfortunately the understanding of Layla and Xcor’s true love and the knowledge of their strong relationship have made a few couples with thorns in their own relationships to face their own insecurities:<br /><br />… Vishous’ insecurity about his love and commitment, about the time Doc Jane spends with him. About how much really Jane cares for him. About how much really V cares for her.<br />… Tohr’s still ongoing issues about his dead wife. Poor Autumn. How can you fight with a ghost for the love of your man?<br />... Blay’s insecurity about being a real father to Qhuinn’s children.<br />… Qhuinn’s insecurity that he is not the only one important for his children. Blay is important, too. Layla is important too. And Qhuinn almost destroys his relationship with Blay. And Qhuinn ends up hating Layla.<br /><br />I have actually talked to a few fans who are not happy with Qhuinn’s behavior and they do not understand it. <br />Well, I totally do understand it! This is just Qhuinn… Emotions run hot with this boy. <br />Let’s not forget that he is just a 30 something years old boy. He is still too young. Just a few years ago, he was getting wasted in the clubs having group sex at the toilets without caring for love and commitment but only for fun and good times. <br />It is not easy for him to be mated and to be a parent.<br />(I still laugh when I remember him a few books ago when he left his keys on his Hammer and someone stole it. It kind of reminds me Qhuinn being locked up in the Cave in this book. Another one of his goofy moments...)<br /><br />Only the story of Trez looks a bit disconnected with the main story, but I have a feeling that the obvious resurrection of Selena is a result of his intense prayer and of Lassiter (the new scribe virgin hahaha) finally losing it and granding Trez’s wish.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I just want her back. I just … I only want Selena back. Please … if there’s anyone up there,<br />help me. Return her to me. I don’t care what form she’s in … I just can’t do this anymore. I can’t live like this for one more fucking night.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />(I am sure that all the readers that have read “The Shadows” were also praying with him!)<br /><br />I have a feeling that the situation with Layla has influenced even Lassiter. Lassiter will confess to Layla about how lost he is now. How much confused he is with his new job.<br /><br />Secondary stories:<br />1.	We are running out of bad guys. An old one is gaining more strength and he is rising. <br /> (Hint: No, not the Omega, Lessers are out of fashion).<br />2.	The Brother’s mansion will be more crowded. Thank God there are enough rooms.<br />3.	The humans keep wondering and searching for the supernatural and for vampires.<br /><br />I am happy with this book. It did not blow my mind, but it was a worthy addition to the series. It did not leave me dissatisfied or angry or sad. It opened doors for many more stories for the series to go stronger. And I have fallen in love with the blind king all over again. I love you Wrath!<br /><br />By the end of the book, I totally respected Layla and her decisions and her determination –almost as much as she started respecting herself:<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Yet she was still alive and she was here. Looking herself in the mirror.<br />And for the first time in her life, she respected what she saw.<br />Bowing to her reflection, she said softly, “Pleased to meet you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />P.S. Thank you so much J.R.Ward :) You rock! <br /><br />-----------------<br />-----------------<br />-----------------<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />5th April 2017<br />I was thinking of starting this book next week, but Ward is having a meeting with the fans next Saturday 8th of April and I am sure after that the Facebook page will be full of spoilers.....<br />So I better start now :)<br /><br />----------------<br />----------------<br /><br />TEASERS FROM THE FACEBOOK PAGE BEFORE PUBLICATION <br /><br />update 31st March 2017<br /><i>Her stress just went out the window as the taste and scent of him became the only thing she knew. </i>, -pg. 373<br />----------------<br />update 29th March 2017<br /><i>I've dreamed of touching you... </i>,-pg. 242<br />----------------<br />update 27th March 2017<br /><i>Destiny had seen fit to give them this one respite.</i>,-pg. 248<br />---------------<br />update 25th March 2017<br /><i>"May I enter your bedroom, female?"</i>,-pg. 243<br />---------------<br />update 23rd March 2017<br /><i>"I am warm in my soul with you before me. That is all I need."</i>, - pg. 157<br />----------------<br />update 21st March 2017<br /><i>His life, such that he was aware of it, was about enduring.</i>,-pg. 98<br /><br />----------------<br />----------------<br /><br />MARCH 2017<br /><i>From out of memory, an image came unto his mind and took his breath away. It was of a tall, slender female in the white robing of the Scribe Virgin’s sacred Chosen. Her blond hair waved down over her shoulders and trailed off at her hips on a gentle breeze, and her eyes were the color of jade, her smile a benediction he had done naught to deserve.<br />The Chosen Layla was what had changed everything for him, recasting the Brotherhood from target to tolerable, from enemy to co–existable tenant in the world.<br />In the short year and a half Xcor had known her, she had had more effect upon his black soul than anyone who had come before, evolving him a greater distance in a lesser time than he would have ever thought possible.</i><br /><br />(Free Chapter 1 excerpt, if you have joined J.R.Ward's emailing list)<br /><br />---------------<br />---------------<br /><br />AUGUST 2016<br />Oh my god, we have a book cover already!<br />I have goosebumps :) I LOVE IT!<br />April 2017 can't come soon enough...<br /><br />---------------<br />---------------<br /><br />APRIL 2016<br />Being a huge fan of "Black Dagger Brotherhood" for a few years now, I cannot stop smiling when a new book is announced and I know for a fact that the stories about the brothers will continue for many more years.<br />Xcor and Layla are definetely not the favourite couple for many series fans, BUT everybody should at least acknowledge that it is a couple that has grown stronger in the last books and they deserve to have their story with either a good ending or a bad ending. <br />We actually already know -especially after "the shadows"- that J R Ward is not afraid to disappoint or surprise her fans and their expectations in order to deliver an ending which is more suited to her vision about this book series. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>
  <a data-text-id="10933063791736713174" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText16780825033603865513" style="display:none">OMG, I just wrote the longest review on this and then hit the freaking power button on my surge protector with my foot on accident and lost everything!!! <div id="review_1730927625" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1730927625" />
    <a title="P " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25327841-p"><img alt="P " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489853536p2/25327841.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1730927625?book_show_action=true">Aug 17, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="P " class="user" itemprop="url" name="P " href="/user/show/25327841-p">P </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25327841-p?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1730927625" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3766034373184134227"><b>
  <blockquote>“Swear to me you will move forward,” he demanded. “I cannot be at peace unless you swear it.”<br/>She put her hands to her face. “I feel as if I am breaking in half.”</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491500555i/22417428.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I liked The Chosen, there was even a moment when I felt it was as good as The Beast or The King, but I just don't like the way all the conflicts are settled, which I will explain later in this review. And the romactic parts of Xcor and Layla weren't that intense - maybe I just expected too much.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491500400i/22417393.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And welcome to the island of self-doubt</span>
  <span id="freeText3766034373184134227" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>“Swear to me you will move forward,” he demanded. “I cannot be at peace unless you swear it.”<br>She put her hands to her face. “I feel as if I am breaking in half.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491500555i/22417428.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I liked The Chosen, there was even a moment when I felt it was as good as The Beast or The King, but I just don't like the way all the conflicts are settled, which I will explain later in this review. And the romactic parts of Xcor and Layla weren't that intense - maybe I just expected too much.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491500400i/22417393.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And welcome to the island of self-doubt of Vishous. Because in this book, we get a free ticket to visit<b>
  <i>V's insecurity</i>
</b> again. Oh god ! I'm so tired of this. Would it be better if we just move on and have other plots instead ? Like Lassister being enigmatic all the time ? Well, all I want to say about this book might be confusing as myself right now. Frankly, I had no idea what would happen before I started reading this book. Xcor and Layla ultimately get their story and I really wanted to see if everything went well for the conflicts being flared since The King; therefore, I was really interested in Xcor even though I felt a bit off with Layla because she's such a whiny character and always holds the story back. And I definitely didn't understand how easy it is for her to change her attitude in an hour and turns herself into a naughty-sexy girl in the bed.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“With all of my black and withered heart, I love you, my female. I deserve not the earth beneath your feet, nor the scent of you in my nose, and never the gift of your blood, but I … I am e’er grateful for the change that you wrought upon me. You have saved me, and the only thing greater than my love for you is my gratitude.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>There are too many POVs in this book: Xcor's, Layla's, Qhuinn's, Blay's, V's, Trez's, Therese's (She's gonna be a big jackpot in the next installment for sure), Thore's, etc. Although I hadn't had any problems with subplots before, I kind of felt everything being slow because of them dragging everything back in this book, especially when a climax comes, the story is cut like that and I had to wait for three or four chapters to finally see what's going on with the characters I was attached to.<br><br>About Xcor and Layla, I've reckoned before a chance for them to be together is all but impossible, and even if they get their HEA, it must be a long road and lots of atonement to be made. But the ending, I just couldn't believe it because <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[it ends with tons of apologies. Xcor and Qhuinn get along very well I couldn't believe what I saw. They even talk about their daughter's future about dating guys while Blay and Layla team up together. It's too good to be true regarding all the drama that gave me headaches. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Just like that, except V's insecuriy that will be a gigantic problem and subplot for the next installment exactly.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491500400ra/22417394.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Not in front of her. Do not do it in front of her if you have any decency. Send her away and then dispatch me.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Qhuinn and Blay's quarreling was unacceptable. I sided with Blay all along when Qhuinn goes crazy and throws a tantrum at Layla who risked her babies with Xcor and kept it a secret. He says something bad to Blay, and if I were him, that would not be easily forgiven. But you know, at the end, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the problems are solved easily like a fairytale with a kiss that can expel everything. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>What I enjoyed was that revelation, it was quite shocking for me to behold because I had no clue about what's bound to transpire. Yet I was made to focus on Wrath since the beginning. His size. His thighs. His shoulders. His biceps. His pec. I didn't take it for granted because it was one of many reasons that sticked me to this series.<br><br>The war is coming to an end. I do hope that I'll live to see the last book of the series, and have an opportunity to read Assail and Trez's story once again.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Fore’ermore, I pledge my allegiance unto to you and yours, serving none other.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491500400i/22417395._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://goo.gl/xhAN2d">https://goo.gl/xhAN2d</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="3766034373184134227" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Ward can keep this series i</span>
  <span id="freeText2683383774688669852" style="display:none">1.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/81237793?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Dark Lover</a> ★★★★★<br>2.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/81237806?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Eternal</a> ★★★★★<br>3.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/81237809?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Awakened</a> ★★★★★<br>4.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/81237801?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Revealed</a> ★★★★★<br>5.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/81237813?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Unbound</a> ★★★★★<br>6.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/81237824?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Enshrined</a> ★★★★<br>7.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/81237822" rel="nofollow noopener">	Lover Avenged</a> ★★★<br>8.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/603024529?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Mine</a> ★★★★<br>9.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/314483063?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Unleashed</a> ★★★<br>10.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/178419300?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Reborn</a> ★★★★<br>11.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/436829415?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover at Last</a> ★★★★★<br>12.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/576338695?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">The King</a> ★★★★★<br>13.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/902921534?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">The Shadows</a> ★★★★★<br>14.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1245980515" rel="nofollow noopener">The Beast</a> ★★★★<br><br><s>Dying</s> Buddy-reading with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1608240169" rel="nofollow noopener">Paloma</a>, because I love her so very much and she writes me name in the old language and warms my heart! ♥:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492720974i/22546591._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Again, I'm dumbfounded by how J.R. Ward can keep this series interesting and how she keeps me so heavily invested after fifteen books! I'm honestly at a loss for words, other than she is truly the PNR master and no one else can really compare. And finally, after what feels like one-hundred- years, <s>the Scribe Virgin</s> we are finally blessed with the long awaited story that belongs to Xcor and Layla. Be still, my heart. <br><br>This all being said, the truth of the matter is that this is book fifteen in a never ending series, therefore <b>
  <u>this review will contain very mild spoilers</u>
</b>! Please, do not continue on if you have not read this book or, more importantly, the fourteen other books leading up to this one! <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“We don’t get to pick who we fall for, and trying to talk yourself out of emotions is a recipe for failure.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Xcor and Layla's story was so worth the wait, and a complete joy to finally read about. The romance was wonderful, the sex was amazing, and the angst felt so very real. It was believable, and heartfelt, and everything I've been anticipating since their story-arc started! <br><br>First and foremost, I hate Qhuinn, I hate Qhuinn, I hate Qhuinn. I hate him with everything I am, and nothing he can ever say in any other BDB book can ever redeem him in my eyes. The things he said to Layla are unforgivable, and I wish for nothing more than for Blay to leave him, but continue to raise the babies with Layla and Xcor while Qhuinn is kicked out of the Brotherhood. When he called Layla an incubator, holy fuck, I legitimately saw red. <br><br>Tohr was also disgusting in this book. His vendetta because of an anniversary didn't even make sense to me, and then, like Qhuinn, the way he treated Layla was completely uncalled for. Can you imagine how these men would feel if some dude spoke to their <i> shellan</i> that way? Like, come on. At least Tohr did redeem himself in the end for me, but it still felt bad that he needed a reason to not be a dickhead. <br><br>Layla got so much emotional abuse in this book; it made me feel sick at times. And that ending, where <i>she</i> apologized back, physically hurt my heart. It was nothing short of disgusting and it just made me hate Qhuinn even more. <br><br>Xcor's backstory was nothing short of heartbreaking. Like, I cried so very hard. The abuse he had to endure, just because of the way he looked, broke me. Xcor's growth is outstanding, and truly the shining light of maybe this entire series. Seeing him see his worth and see that he is worthy of love is something I can't even put into words.<br><br>Also, can we take a minute to say how amazing it is that J.R. Ward has a main character with a birth defect, which is actually a very common birth defect that is never talked about, especially in PNR or just romance in general? I love how she showcases Xcor's birth defect, but never makes him his birth defect. J.R. Ward seriously knocks it out of the park when it comes to diversity, and she never stops impressing me. And Xcor is bae. <br><br>Wrath was the MVP of this book, besides Xcor and Layla, obviously. Wrath always saw reason, even if Beth was helping to guide him, and always did what was right. He is truly king for a reason, and I loved him so much in this book! Seriously, he was everything. <br><br>And Beth, oh Beth! What a fucking Queen! She is everything and truly the glue that holds the entire mansion together. Her and Fitz, I'm telling you, without one of them the BDB would completely explode.<br><br>My other favorite was Lassiter! Oh, that boy is going to have some explaining to do in the next book. His personality is exactly what the Brotherhood needs, and he was seriously amazing in this book, especially that crazy ending. <br><br>Like, I know I just didn't read and obsess over <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1245980515" rel="nofollow noopener">The Beast</a> to not hear anything else about Bitty in this book! Where the hell were Mary and Rhage? Seriously, I was so sad that they were pretty much MIA this entire book. <br><br>And Assail and Sola! Where is this good, good, good angst at? All we got to see was Assail still healing, but, Lord, I need glimpses of their story-arc to get me by. <br><br>John Matthew was only mentioned in this book one time, but since he is by far my least favorite Brother, I was completely okay with it. <br><br>Saxton made a couple cameos, and I loved every time he was mentioned, but every time I was pretty much just screaming into my book about how Blay should be with him and not gross fucking Qhuinn. I can't wait to see what J.R. Ward has in store for Saxton's story, though, because I don't feel as confident about the him and Throe OTP as I was in the last book.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“There is nothing wrong in this world or the next in finding out your own power.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I feel like Vishous and Jane are going to split. Which doesn't really make sense, because they bonded, right? Like, we have been taught for fourteen books that there is no power on Earth stronger than a bonded male, but Vishous doesn't seem to care at all anymore. He played such a big role in this book, too, and I think it's just setting up for him to have a brand new story line and probably a brand new lover.<br><br>As much as I love the Shadows, I'm not sure how much I love this Selena recantation story line. I'm on the fence about it, but hopefully it feels better as it progresses. Also, Trez better be kissing the ground Lassiter is walking on. Seriously, what a fucking bro. <br><br>I loved seeing all the brothers, all the friendships, and all the wonderful dynamics that make the Black Dagger Brotherhood what it is. I am seriously so invested in this bunch of warrior vampires, it's unreal. I cried happy and sad tears so much throughout this book, I was such a hot mess, and I am not sure how I'm going to be able to wait for the next installment. <br><br>Yet, my inner pervert wants to say that there wasn't enough sex in this book for my liking. I mean, what was in this book was amazing, but it just seemed sparser than the average BDB book, in my very perverted opinion. <br><br>Also, at this point there are so many freaking points of view that it is actually insane. Like, it is not a problem for me, and I always remember who is who, but sometimes I sit back and think about all these people and I'm just like, "damn!" And just think, we will probably be getting six new points of view very soon! <br><br>My biggest problem with this book was the sexist things that kept happening, especially to poor, undeserving Layla. I understand that this book series has been built for years and years around the definition of pure alpha males, and I'm okay with that, but this book made the brothers do and say some very questionable things that had me very upset. If you could take out the sexism, this book would be a five star book, unquestionable. Yet, I can't unsee (<i>or unfeel</i>) it, so here we are. <br><br>I also understand that we as a society have a problem with identifying things/items with gender (i.e., little girls like pink bows and little boys like blue trucks), but the way Qhuinn spoke about the twins made me pretty pissed off. And everyone saying how Rhampage was a little warrior constantly, but how beautiful, perfect, and undateable Lyric was just grossed me out. Oh how far we've come, but oh how far we still need to go.<br><br>Okay, so that ending! Did it feel a little strange to anyone else? Like, is J.R. Ward going to time skip up ahead with the kids? I completely love reading about the younger generation in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1244182490" rel="nofollow noopener">Black Dagger Legacy</a>, but this book ending left me a little shook. Hopefully I'm just reading into things, but I'm super curious to see what J.R. Ward is going to do next. Regardless, I do trust her. <br><br>J.R. Ward is amazing, and I hope she keeps this series going forever, because I know I will keep reading for as long as she writes them. I'm so happy that Xcor and Layla finally got the happy ending that they have deserved for a long while and through very many books. And like I said above, I can't wait to see where J.R. Ward decides to take this series next!<br><br> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The Chosen Layla was what had changed everything for him”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><a href="https://meltotheany.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://meltotheany.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany/profile" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a></span>
