    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1962999688" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1962999688" />
    <a title="Jen Davis" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis"><img alt="Jen Davis" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1548427639p2/4669344.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1962999688?book_show_action=true">Apr 05, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen Davis" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen Davis" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis">Jen Davis</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1962999688" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9123857642568414328">I know a lot of BDB fans were not excited for this book. JR Ward alienated so many people (myself included) with the ending of The Shadows, and frankly, a lot of people hate Layla. I hated Layla for a long time, so I get that. But I actually was looking forward to this book because I love a tortured hero and I’m all about forbidden romance. I’ve kinda been burning for this pairing for years. <br/><br/>There were things I liked in this story, but a great deal that I didn’t. I’m going to talk about the plot</span>
  <span id="freeText9123857642568414328" style="display:none">I know a lot of BDB fans were not excited for this book. JR Ward alienated so many people (myself included) with the ending of The Shadows, and frankly, a lot of people hate Layla. I hated Layla for a long time, so I get that. But I actually was looking forward to this book because I love a tortured hero and I’m all about forbidden romance. I’ve kinda been burning for this pairing for years. <br /><br />There were things I liked in this story, but a great deal that I didn’t. I’m going to talk about the plot some, so if you haven’t read the book and you want to stay entirely spoiler free, consider yourself warned. My main problem with this book was that Ward set up the conflict with the utter annihilation of Qhuinn’s character. I’m not saying <em>Qhuinn makes bad choices.</em> I’m saying, <em>I hated Qhuinn. I wanted to set Qhuinn on fire. Qhuinn was unrecognizable from the character we’ve known in all the books leading up to this one.</em> That is not ok. He’s not just an ass. He is cruel, violent, and vindictive. He is beyond horrible to Layla, and frankly, speaks to Blay in a way that is completely at odds with the devoted mate he has always been up until now. Ward turned this character into something else to force the story where she wanted it to go and I am not down with that.<br /><br />I’m also disappointed that Xcor and Layla start the book already in love. Yes, we’ve had a ton of building in previous books but I wanted the money scene where they finally reveal their feelings, and (especially for Xcor) it’s earth shattering and we get that big FINALLY moment. Their love was a given and I felt cheated. Don’t get me wrong, they are lovely together. I felt their desperation over their stolen moments and their abiding love, which is something Ward gets right. I just wish we would’ve had a big moment when they put their feelings out there for the first time.<br /><br />As you know, these days Ward is all about the subplots, none of which I cared for. I especially Hated Trez’s story with a Selena lookalike. Hated with a capital H. I hated Tohr’s backslide. And I was completely unmoved by V’s emotional disconnect from Doc Jane. I had to fight the urge to skim often in the side scenes, when I wasn’t contemplating throwing my ereader in frustration.<br /><br />I am interested in anything to do with the Band of Bastards. And the flashback scenes with Xcor broke my heart. Poor Xcor. He reminds of Zsadist. (Who I miss, BTW.) Such a gentle soul who has endured so much misery. I love how Layla changes him. He is so good to her! So heartbreakingly devoted and utterly in love with her. It's so lovely how she sees him... as a good man and a warrior. And I enjoyed her finding her own identity. <br /><br />I also thought the big climax scene was pretty awesome.<br /><br />But the resolution was super-rushed and way too easy. Especially when it came to Qhuinn. As much as Ward turned his character on a dime at the beginning, she did it just as quickly at the end. It felt shallow and unsatisfying.<br /><br />Overall, I found the book very uneven. It had some really satisfying moments. But just as many disappointments.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9123857642568414328" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1605519700?book_show_action=true">Apr 09, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carolina Carriço" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carolina Carriço" href="/user/show/14877543-carolina-carri-o">Carolina Carriço</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1605519700" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18394106023217206442"><i>*spoilers*</i><br/><br/><b>After reading the book :</b><br/><br/>As I expected I absolutely loved <b>Xcor</b> in this book. I fell in love with wayyyyyy back and I was looking forward to his book and with high expectations. Even though some details in his relationship with Layla wasn't my idea of perfection, it all worked out.<br/>Speaking of the lady of this book, I was never her biggest fan but she managed to surprise me and earn my respect. She was a badass mother and fearless defender of her mate. You did your job well, Layla.<br/><br/>Despite</span>
  <span id="freeText18394106023217206442" style="display:none"><i>*spoilers*</i><br /><br /><b>After reading the book :</b><br /><br />As I expected I absolutely loved <b>Xcor</b> in this book. I fell in love with wayyyyyy back and I was looking forward to his book and with high expectations. Even though some details in his relationship with Layla wasn't my idea of perfection, it all worked out.<br />Speaking of the lady of this book, I was never her biggest fan but she managed to surprise me and earn my respect. She was a badass mother and fearless defender of her mate. You did your job well, Layla.<br /><br />Despite all this there were a few things that really <b>disappointed</b> me or left me confused. Let's start with the most obvious one. <br /><b>Qhuinn</b>, I found his behavior through out the book so out of character and mostly annoying. Not to speak it was excessive considering the outcome of the situation. It was just...<i>ugh</i>. Thank God for Blay for being so level headed and dealing with everything like a champ. <br /><br />Second was Throe. Everything about his chapter was, first of all boring AF, second ridiculous and absurd. How the hell with the author explain <i>that</i>? It feels so foreign in this world of vampires and lessers.<br /><br />Third and lastly, my precious baby <b>Vishous</b>. If he wasn't the love of my life, my sun and stars, my favorite character in the universe I'd be hating his guts, considering all this I still want to kick his one ball, have Rhage and Butch hand him his ass and put him in therapy. He's absolutely fucked up and is going to put himself in the worst shit. Is it possible that his paternal instinct is kicking in?! And since Jane can't have kids...well everything? It's a possibility, but not an excuse. Never a fucking excuse for his thoughts and behavior. I'm hoping next book will be about him. And he will get his head straight again so I can add book #16 to my favorites.<br /><br />Even with all this <i>small</i> things, the main story about Layla and Xcor met my expectations, as mentioned above, therefore the four star rating. And I can't forget to talk about the end. That was worth it all annoyances and disappointments! I loved seeing everyone working together. I loved seeing the <i>'three fathers, one mother, two babies'</i> part. And I loved the prediction for Lyrac's future. As long as Ward sets her head straight and stops messing with everyone's personalities and adding useless bullshit to the story, everything will work just fine, and I will just keep on loving these books with all my heart and soul.<br /><br />PS. Lassiter is the fucking best. I love him so fucking much. Seeing him in this book dealing with everything made me tear up and want to hug him tight until all hope was returned to him.<br /><br />------------<br /><br /><b>Don't read it if you want to go into the next books completely blind!</b><br /><br /><br />Some important news:<br />- Lash will eventually come back.<br />- Lassiter will have a book. And he's the Virgin successor.<br />- Bitty's uncle will probably show up before the 6 month time is over.<br />- There will be crossover between BDB and Fallen Angels.<br />- Warden wants to write a book about Nalla finding love.<br />- Saxton is having his own HEA.<br />- The Virgin won't have her own book.<br />- Blay and John are joining the Brotherhood. And Payne possibly as well.<br />- Xcor already redeemed himself. Nobody knows yet how tho.<br />- Throe's sister might or might now be dead.<br />- Sola has met a guy. Assail has no idea.<br />- No HEA for Havers. Warden hates his guts.<br />- She doesn't see a kid for Butch. Yet.<br />- Phury's kid will come back.<br />- She's writing another Insider's Guide. And she would like to write some stories in the Brother's past.<br />- No one will ever know about the Darius/John connection.<br />- Payne is up to something. She hasn't been around as much.<br />- No book for Fritz.<br /><br /><b>Full transcript</b>: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/JRWardBooks/posts/10153547395808231">https://www.facebook.com/JRWardBooks/...</a></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1605431806" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2976511590668690464">First, that cover? No.<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492055776i/22477387._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Much better. <br/>(<i>Please don't steal or edit this artwork. Thankies!</i>)<br/><br/><b>Xcor</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491949251ra/22466094.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Layla</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491949833i/22466182._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491949833ra/22466183.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>*sigh*<br/><br/>Second, let me start with what I enjoyed and talk about the featured couple since they deserve the praise and attention that other things seemed to have eclipsed and overshadowed them with.<br/><br/><b>Xcor & Layla</b><br/>Lovely, sweet, beautiful, honest, brave, fearless. Funny how they have been pitted as the ‘underdogs’ and ‘bad guys’ by both the Brotherhood and readers alike who have hated this couple and yet the</span>
  <span id="freeText2976511590668690464" style="display:none">First, that cover? No.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492055776i/22477387._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Much better. <br>(<i>Please don't steal or edit this artwork. Thankies!</i>)<br><br><b>Xcor</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491949251ra/22466094.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Layla</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491949833i/22466182._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491949833ra/22466183.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*sigh*<br><br>Second, let me start with what I enjoyed and talk about the featured couple since they deserve the praise and attention that other things seemed to have eclipsed and overshadowed them with.<br><br><b>Xcor &amp; Layla</b><br>Lovely, sweet, beautiful, honest, brave, fearless. Funny how they have been pitted as the ‘underdogs’ and ‘bad guys’ by both the Brotherhood and readers alike who have hated this couple and yet they managed to show up and out how honorable, selfless, brave and LOYAL they both are. HA. These two showed more spine, strength, integrity and heart than the apparent ‘good guys’ in here. I was so proud of the both of them, how they stood their ground on their own and for each other. Layla especially. Go girl! Seeing her literally go nose-to-nose with snarling Brothers for her children AND the man she loves was just everything. Wooh! Standing ovation right there. She went even beyond what I was expecting for Xcor. I loved how she had Xcor’s back through everything and went all lioness mode over him. Team Xcorla for the win! I'm happy they got their HEA and overcame the impossible. And I didn't realize Xcor is so poetic with his words. :P I also really loved all the different angles Ward built up to show Xcor is redeemed and could be forgiven by the Brothers. I was worried it would be too quick and easy and contrived but it wasn't. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I have dreamed of touching you,” he murmured. “So many times I have…” <br>
</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><b>Wrath</b><br>My boo. My man. My #1. Shout out to him! He still continues to be badass and a wonderful King. Your favs could neva! He showed so much integrity, compassion, firmness, and was the freaking calm in this sh*t storm. There were some serious laugh out loud moments with him and I will forever love the visual of Wrath physically muzzling V and going for his throat to shut him up. GOLD. STAR. MOMENT.<br><br><b>Phury</b><br>Phury!!!! Cormia!!! Long time no see! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462309307ra/18980545.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Lassiter</b><br>He’s already taking his role of SV very seriously and I love that. To see him be brought to his knees--literally--was great to see. Adds another layer to this character. <br><br><b>Blay</b> <br>I love you. You are too good, kind, patient and loving to have to put up with this ish. <br><br><b>Tohr</b><br>Yes Tohr had his ragey dickhead moments in here (when it rains it pours apparently) but witnessing the hopeful tentative shocked awe of discovering you aren't so alone anymore and have blooded family was beautiful to see. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>With a halting series of ungainly movements, Xcor held onto the male's shoulders and pushed himself back a little. Meeting Tohrment in the eye, he whispered, "My brother." <br>"Yes," the male said hoarsely, a sheen of tears making that blue stare glow like a pair of sapphires. "I am your brother."<br>It was hard to say who embraced who, but suddenly they were both holding on, one upon another, warrior to warrior.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Yes I'm still upset with him and the whole Wellsie mourning. Cut it out dude. <br><br>Now onto the big, bad and ugly.....<br><br><b>Qhuinn</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491981022ra/22468593.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Oy. Qhuinn did you lose your fucking mind? Ward did the most with him. I just don't understand why she thought going this far was redeemable or even realistic. In fact the only thing it managed to bring home is that Qhuinn still has a lot of growing up to do. A LOT. Going around trigger happy and acting like a homicidal lunatic just because your ass felt betrayed is not a good enough reason. Sorry but nope. Blay deserved better. Qhuay deserved better. She made him into a raging abusive psycho for unfair extreme reasons. His blind sense of self-entitlement and victimhood was truly astounding. I was prepared and expecting him to go off like a canon in here. But how he went off? Hell no. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ You threatened to kill the mother of your child, called her a lying whore, pointed a gun at your mate, denounced his role as a father, pointed a gun at the mother of your child <i><b>while she was holding your babies.</b></i> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> And yet you can't get over Layla putting your unborn young in *possible* danger?? Take your own advice asswipe. I don’t care how emotional you are, your actions and words are your own. Own it. And the fact that he was favoring Rhamp over Lyric because she happens to look just like her mother just proves he has no business being a father. I found this so disgusting and unconscionable. My biggest problem was that it took Qhuinn too long to see reason. His “I don’t owe anyone shit” petty attitude through most of this really stank and was just asking for a throat punch. It made what was already really bad, just worse. Grow up dude. Grow the fuck up. I expected better from you. And I didn't appreciate how everyone around Qhuinn let him act like a fucking child just because he's shook up over protecting his young. Bullshit. Wrath should have kicked him out of the Brotherhood. Period. I don't understand how waving a gun around your kids and on your mate is excusable.<br><br>If Phury could get kicked out for his smoking problem and slashing up bad guys, then so the fuck could Qhuinn for <b>threatening his loved ones with a damn gun</b>. The nonstop coddling over this character is fucking insane. <br><br>And as much as I love Layla, I still think giving Qhuinn children was a <b>huge</b> mistake on Ward’s part. I’ve been saying this from the start and I stand by it now. Qhuinn is not grown enough or stable to raise 2 kids. He's still a child. Sorry but that's the damn truth. All this shit that went down here is perfect example of why. And good for Blay for laying down the law and showing some serious tough love. I honestly wish Blay had taken those kids as his own legally. *shrugs* #YesISaidIt #TeamBlay That's honestly how this should have ended. Blay taking those kids and Qhuinn working on redeeming himself and figuring things out with Xcor. This seriously effected my Qhuay love. The whole time I felt sorry for Blay for having to put up with his bullshit again. I'm not sure I can enjoy this couple anymore after this. Ward still has major work to do to redeem Qhuinn in my eyes. This should <i>not</i> have been resolved in this book, no way. It's too much and too soon to sweep under the rug. And as much as I love that Xcor was pardoned and welcomed by the BDB family, it happened too quickly and unrealistically for my liking. The ending was the most slapstick convoluted thing out of this entire book. How someone goes from near homicidal rage towards someone then to fist bumping besties in a matter of <i>days</i> is beyond me. I didn't buy it. Qhuinn should have been begrudgingly making truce w/ Layla and Xcor (just for Blay), not acting buddy buddy with Xcor. Ridiculous. If anything that was the most OCC moment for both Xcor and Qhuinn. It was one too many extra cherries on the sundae. <br><br><b>Vishous</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491954755ra/22466626.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Vishous I'm really tired of your ass. I really am. *sigh* We are back to this again? Really? Sorry Ward but I ain’t buying it. I know you know you are full of sh*t with this one. Even your Rice Krispies have receipts and what you are saying now does not line up to what you have said and WROTE in the series and yes even prior to V and Butch’s books. Try Book 1 Dark Lover. So please spare me with the fan-flaming ‘omg the publishers made me do it! I never evah wanted Vishous with Jane’ pot stirring. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1493051440ra/22578774.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Let me first be clear and say I'm reacting more to what Ward said at her book signing than what was teased in this book. V hasn't done anything damaging......<i>yet</i>. But he's crossing that line quickly. He's right now all up in his head and feeling disconnected with Jane because she's always working at the clinic all the time (how is she always that busy though?) and he's feeling ignored. He's contemplating cheating. Someone explain to me how a <b>bonded</b> male can cheat much less even contemplate cheating? It goes against their nature and the rules of bonding. Hey asshole how about TALK TO YOUR WIFE if you are feeling a certain way instead of fingering your phone for possible hookups. His passive aggressive 'my mama didn't love me and my mate is too busy for me' emo shit is disgusting. I'm so over him. Grow that testicle back you are so clearly missing. <br><br>Here's my confession: I never liked or cared for V. To me he was always a cold, vain, emotionally stunted asshole. But with Jane, he came alive, she humanized him and made him feel. She made me care. I loved their story so much. It was raw, honest, emotional and unforgiving (and sexy AF too). And Ward already tried a revisit with these two in Lover Unleashed and it was one big clusterfuck contrived mess. Now she seems determined to mess with them again and I'm not sure there will be anything left of them worth salvaging and that really bothers me. Fuck that. Jane deserves better. I deserve better. You may just systematically destroy one of your strongest pairings, and strongest works for more contrived angst to sell a story, and what a shame. Lover Unbound was damn good and one of the best books of this series. I will pray for Jane cause she sure as shit deserves better than this roughshod treatment. <br><br>And Ward I thought Zsadist was your favorite and you hated V? Now suddenly you love him?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491980254ra/22468562.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>How convenient.<br><br><b>Xcor/Layla</b><br>Yup you are seeing double and no it's not a mistake. As much I loved these two's sweet moments, I felt they took a backseat in here. A reader's biggest fear when going into a book they highly anticipate about a couple they love is the star couple not getting the attention they deserve. And that's pretty much what happened here. I didn't feel like enough time was spent on them, what scenes they had were too short and abrupt. And yes I would have liked longer sex scenes. The hot factor was completely missing and Ward played it so safe for reasons I don't understand. Oh that's right, she was too busy fucking around with Qhuinn and V's man pain to do these two justice. 😒 Layla is a freaking Ehros for crying out loud! USE IT. And all that emotional angst and tension that played out so beautifully in the previous books just seemed to evaporate in here, so I found some of their scenes a bit anticlimactic and unexciting. That sense of slow burn, urgency and anticipation was completely missing. I still loved their scenes but they came off very tame. <br><br><b>Trez &amp; Therese</b><br>What is the point? Talk about jumping the gun. I’m already over these two I’m sorry to say. Too soon. Way too soon Ward. This could have had potential…..down the road. But the delivery here was so premature, gimmicky and anti-climactic. Readers already know it's Selena. So where is the surprise in this? And how is this even gonna work? Trez will know it’s Selena but she won’t? Excuse me but finding out a guy is crazy for you because you are the spitting image of his dead mate is a total mood killer. What was the point of The Shadows then? Some things should honestly be left alone. This just screams course correction, scrambling to fix a mistake. Slapping a band aid on it isn't gonna help Ward. (And BTW: we go from "my dog died so Selena had to die-----&gt;blame it on the Rice Krispies!-----&gt; Lassiter brings her back as a "gift" because the SV left"????........Absurd.)<br><br><b>The timeline</b><br>This is by far the biggest pet peeve of mine when it comes to over-arcing series. Ward did the same thing in her FA series and it drove me nuts. Why the f*ck would you have your story unfold in only a matter of 3 DAYS in one book when there is so much that needs to be covered?? What's the rush? This isn't fan fiction or a Slice of Life. There is literally <b>no reason</b> for this entire book to only cover 3 days when you are talking about your main character needing to be fully redeemed, pardoned and saved from dying. Absurd. And being reminded of it in the last chapter is like a house of cards getting blown down all at once. It makes the entire story come off comical, flat and so unrealistic. Yes the hero and heroine already fell in love before this book, that doesn't matter. Xcor should have been the primary focus here and the timeline should have taken weeks, at the very <i>least</i>. Not 3 fucking days of everyone acting like lunatics and passing out "I'm sowies" at the very end. Nah. <br><br>Moral(s) of the story here: Don't make all your characters into flaming assholes and some things are better left alone.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="2976511590668690464" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1953110672" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1953110672" />
    <a title="❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5205999-dorsey-aka-wrath-lover-reviews"><img alt="❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1485279859p2/5205999.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1953110672?book_show_action=true">Mar 26, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️" href="/user/show/5205999-dorsey-aka-wrath-lover-reviews">❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook " href="/book/show/35229231-the-chosen">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5205999-dorsey-aka-wrath-lover-reviews?shelf=audio_books">audio_books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1953110672" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer553032972006298857"><b>*** WARNING: THIS REVIEW CONTAINS SPOILERS!!***</b> <br/><br/><i>
  <b>3.5 Deceitful Chosen Stars!!</b>
</i><br/><br/>Sooooo…..I’m going to break this down by storylines (and there are many) as I did with the last couple of books.<br/><br/><b>Layla and Xcor</b><br/>I was waiting what seems like forever for their story, whether you like them or not, or you just wanted to be done with them we waited a loooooong time!! Xcor, admittedly was not good guy, we find out that he suffered as a young boy, teen, and young adult and then throw in the Blood Letter fin</span>
  <span id="freeText553032972006298857" style="display:none"><b>*** WARNING: THIS REVIEW CONTAINS SPOILERS!!***</b> <br><br><i>
  <b>3.5 Deceitful Chosen Stars!!</b>
</i><br><br>Sooooo…..I’m going to break this down by storylines (and there are many) as I did with the last couple of books.<br><br><b>Layla and Xcor</b><br>I was waiting what seems like forever for their story, whether you like them or not, or you just wanted to be done with them we waited a loooooong time!! Xcor, admittedly was not good guy, we find out that he suffered as a young boy, teen, and young adult and then throw in the Blood Letter finding and claiming him as his son those experiences hardened him and I have to say as much as I hated him (he did attempt to kill Wrath!!) I felt an overwhelming compassion for him. Layla was just as irritating as she has been in the last few books, I am not a fan of hers, but, I must say she was fearless mother and champion for Xcor.<br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/BDB/PicsArt_1491552834958_zpsqgtxmpm5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491558244i/22421819.jpg" alt=" photo PicsArt_1491552834958_zpsqgtxmpm5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Quinn and Blay</b><br>Quinn was a <b>
  <i>total and complete asshole</i>
</b> throughout pretty much the whole book, he was an asshole to Blay, Layla, the King…… and pretty much anyone who got in his way (except Blay's parents, who are freaking awesome!). The thing is, I totally understand where his emotion was coming from, but, I felt that emotion should have been directed at Layla and Layla alone. I admired him for his devotion to Wrath, and the brotherhood. Xcor is the Enemy and that emotion should have been acknowledged….<i>
  <b>by everyone</b>
</i>!! I know a lot of readers now hate him...not me. I just keep thinking of everything he’s done for everyone in the past, to name a few.....<br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/BDB/FD4BF018-2A31-4DDC-91AA-19B6FE8CB80E_zpsiw5yxvwb.jpeg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1521957470i/25270584.jpg" alt=" photo FD4BF018-2A31-4DDC-91AA-19B6FE8CB80E_zpsiw5yxvwb.jpeg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I’m not happy that J.R. Ward chose to throw him under the bus....completely sucks that someone everyone loved is now <b>hated</b>, heartbreaking. <br><br>Blay tried to play peacemaker to keep “his family” together and Qhuinn lashed out at him during the confrontation with Layla upon learning of her relationship with Xcor. Yes, Qhinn went too far, but, Blay should have been more understanding upon learning the depths Layla’s deceptions…and in my opinion offered support to Q. In the end, everything worked out but it seemed like a lot of unnecessary drama.<br><br><b>Tohr</b><br>Torhment is still missing his Wellsie and still grieving at times, in this case her birthday. He still has bad moments and a pain that won’t go away. Autumn is a good mate to him and doesn’t seem to resent the time and emotion given to his first mate....I wonder how long that will last? He also learns of his family ties to Xcor and we’re shown how torn he is about having a blooded brother and seeking the vengeance promised him by Wrath.<br><br><b>Throe</b><br>Throe is going to be a force to be reckoned with in future books….I’m still not sure what power he has, and more importantly from whom, it’s all bad and scary evil!!!<br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/BDB/PicsArt_1491556033409_zpshcx3cetz.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491558244i/22421820.jpg" alt=" photo PicsArt_1491556033409_zpshcx3cetz.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Trez</b><br>If you follow JR Ward, you already knew this was happening ("Do you believe in reincarnation, because Trez will"…). We're introduced to Therese, a young woman (vampire) who goes to Sal’s seeking a job, i’Am is blown away by her resemblance to Selena. Naturally, Trez sees her and is drawn to her as much as he tries to stay away……I'm looking forward to seeing how this storyline develops.<br><br><b>V and Jane</b><br>Trouble is brewing and they are definitely growing apart, Doc Jane is extremely busy in the clinic with very little time for her mate and V is resenting it…..which turns out not to be a good thing as his mind starts to wonder. We are left hanging on the issue which I have a feeling we’ll get in the next <i>Black Dagger Legacy</i> book.<br><br><b>Lastly, we come to our favorite Fallen Angel Lassiter </b><br>The Scribe Virgin has named Lassiter as her successor. I’m definitely looking forward to the brothers finding out, and I can’t wait to see what crazy ideas Lassiter has in store for the brothers.<br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/BDB/PicsArt_1481279546701_zpsfjvk276f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481786200i/21454469.jpg" alt=" photo PicsArt_1481279546701_zpsfjvk276f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Final thoughts……</b><br>All-in-all, I enjoyed this book for the most part, but, I have to say the ending to the Q/Blay/Layla/Xcor storyline left a bad taste in my mouth….and tell me why did they (Q, Blay, &amp; Xcor) all have to turn into a bunch of pansyasses in end….really WARDen? Where were the shitkicker badasses we know and love!? I was totally unprepared for the sappy lovefest they had going on. And really, did you have to throw Qhinn under the bus like that? Throughout the whole series he's been a loyal friend and brother, he's absolutely steadfast in his loyalty and unselfish to a fault....now (from the reviews I've read on Goodreads) he's <b>hated</b> by fans of the series for remaining <b>
  <i>loyal</i>
</b> to the Brotherhood (unlike Layla)<i>
  <b>so f*ing disappointing</b>
</i>!! <br><br>All the rest, I’m happy with. As always, I'm looking forward to more of my beloved King Wrath and the rest of the Brotherhood.<br><br><br><b>*Audio book reread on March 24th, 2018</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="553032972006298857" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5349316680155418616">Actual trash.<br/><br/>I'm not even gonna bother hashing this one out.<br/><br/>A few reviews that mention some of my grievances <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1606479670?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>here</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1963329144?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>here</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1961990892?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>here</a>.<br/><br/>After 15 books, plus ten thousand spin-offs it comes as a surprise to me that I think this is where I'm gonna quit it.   <span id="freeText5349316680155418616" style="display:none">Actual trash.<br /><br />I'm not even gonna bother hashing this one out.<br /><br />A few reviews that mention some of my grievances <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1606479670?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1963329144?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1961990892?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a>.<br /><br />After 15 books, plus ten thousand spin-offs it comes as a surprise to me that I think this is where I'm gonna quit it. But enduring verbal and almost physical abuse from the co-parent of your children is where I draw the line with how much I can stand of Ward's blatant mistreatment of women. And I say that while being a huge fan of Qhuinn's character (before this book) and actually not liking Layla.<br /><br />Not to mention the absolute obliteration of the rules of a paranormal world that have been shoved down our throats for FIFTEEN books. It's been a weary and tiring and not at all good journey. I hope this series ends (ha! the joke's on me) with everyone and their mother getting killed. They all deserve it.<br /><br />Final note: I can't believe that this is the last I'll ever read about one of my favourite couples of the series:<br /><blockquote>
  <p>"V thought for a moment she would notice that he was walking away and come after him. But she didn't."</p>
</blockquote><br /><br />That's crap. This book is crap. These last few instalments of the series have been crap.<br /><br /><b>Hasta nunca BDB, creo que ahora sí llegué a mi límite. Y ésta serie se puede ir a la verga.</b><br /><br />*Edit* This link takes you to the transcript of the Q&amp;A for the signing event of The Chosen. It answers some questions in case anyone is interested. <span id="freeTextContainer7366604350282745678">3 stars - Paranormal Romance<br/><br/>I'm so conflicted with this review because there were definitely some extremely disappointing, WTF moments worthy of a 1-star review and numerous characters and events that royally pissed me off. It's a real shame Ward's doing such a disservice to her loyal readers/fans by betraying some of the intrinsic principles of the Black Dagger Brotherhood. And OMG, Ward's extreme rambling, irrelevant details, and excessive minutiae drove me nuts! <br/><br/>I've honestly never really bee</span>
  <span id="freeText7366604350282745678" style="display:none">3 stars - Paranormal Romance<br><br>I'm so conflicted with this review because there were definitely some extremely disappointing, WTF moments worthy of a 1-star review and numerous characters and events that royally pissed me off. It's a real shame Ward's doing such a disservice to her loyal readers/fans by betraying some of the intrinsic principles of the Black Dagger Brotherhood. And OMG, Ward's extreme rambling, irrelevant details, and excessive minutiae drove me nuts! <br><br>I've honestly never really been a big Qhuinn fan, and I've always thought Blay deserved so much better. But I absolutely HATED Qhuinn in this! There was no forgiving him or redeeming him for me after what he said/did. Nope! And Vishous? WTF? The whole Trez/Selena/<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Theresa <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> storyline is really confusing and frustrating. <br><br>Layla's always annoyed me, but she grew some much needed backbone in this. I was kind of blah/meh about her and Xcor, but their romance ended up being so much better than I expected. But I didn't believe how everything got wrapped up all nice, neat, and tidy with a freaking bow on it so lightning fast right at the end, especially after dragging it all out for so long. <br><br>I loved Wrath and Lassiter in this, and the audiobook narrator was fabulous!<br><br>Otherwise, here's pretty much a summary of how I felt while reading this:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494037645ra/22678562.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494037499ra/22678548.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474569117ra/20617640.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494037951i/22678582.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1827780783" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12940165418050402590"><b>Solid 2.75 Stars</b><br/><br/>Yes, had to change my rating from 3.25 stars :(<br/><br/>Okay.. So I attempted my re-read, I got to chapter 38 and decided I knew exactly how I felt about this book. First, let me start with the odd things that I liked. This won't take long considering there's only one thing that I wasn't totally upset or confused about..<br/><br/><i>
  <b>Trez/"Selena"/Therese</b>
</i><br/>I was not happy AT ALL when I learned that after all the heart wrenching Ward caused me in the <i>"Shadows"</i>, that she was actually bringing <i>Selena</i> ba</span>
  <span id="freeText12940165418050402590" style="display:none"><b>Solid 2.75 Stars</b><br /><br />Yes, had to change my rating from 3.25 stars :(<br /><br />Okay.. So I attempted my re-read, I got to chapter 38 and decided I knew exactly how I felt about this book. First, let me start with the odd things that I liked. This won't take long considering there's only one thing that I wasn't totally upset or confused about..<br /><br /><i>
  <b>Trez/"Selena"/Therese</b>
</i><br />I was not happy AT ALL when I learned that after all the heart wrenching Ward caused me in the <i>"Shadows"</i>, that she was actually bringing <i>Selena</i> back, and so quickly. <b>THE NERVE!</b> But amazingly, this angle in this book, was the only thing that I liked and had absolutely no issue about where it appears to be going. I love <i>Trez</i>. I hate that he's suffering and I found that I just want him happy. I hope it turns out well and unfolds in a way that's beautiful, intense, &amp; real.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>Xcor &amp; Layla</b>
</i><br />*Le Sigh* Now I for one have been in love with <i>Xcor</i> since I met him waaaay back in <i>Payne's</i> book. Didn't want to love him, but hey, he got me. In that book it was clear to me then, at least where part of his story was going to land. And we FINALLY see those fruits in this book (He and Tohr), but I was highly disappointed with the lack of <b>PASSION</b>, push and pull, &amp; intensity between <i>Xcor and Layla</i>. I mean come on WARD! Where was it?! All the intense, stolen moments in the past with these two was not even a blip on the pages here. I LOVED the devotion and sweetness between these two, because yes, we needed that. But I needed a balance here. These two were finally able to be together, but with the enormous threat of being ripped apart for so many MAJOR reasons. And none of that intensity or passion or fire was present here. In or out of the bedroom. So <i>this chick</i> here, was found wanting. MAJORLY wanting. #IFeelSoCheated.. *hangs head*<br /><br />Now, I've always understood and liked <i>Layla</i>. Even when she <i>appeared</i> to be just a blank slate in the beginning. I got her. Every book she has been in, has confirmed my first impressions of her. She's growth personified. I'm proud of her. She gets stronger every time I see her :)<br /><br /><i>Xcor's</i> back story I wanted more of this. I can't lie about that either. I felt like we were just given the <i>"Headlines"</i> &amp; not the true <i>"Meat"</i> of the story. Still, what I got broke my heart and allowed me to get a little more insight into him. Why &amp; how he became who he became. And also how he could turn away from his initial road of darkness, destruction, &amp; hate; for the love of a good woman.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>Xcor &amp; Tohr</b>
</i> The moment of reveals for these two was beautiful. I can't deny that. But I needed more. It all happened very late in the game. So it gave the feel of emotions, revelations, &amp; acceptance of coming too quickly. It was rushed, and I didn't like that at all.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>Qhuinn &amp; Blay</b>
</i><br />I felt like their issues were warranted, but I felt more from them, than the main couple of this book. They sort of stole the show. I thought it was beautiful, heartbreaking and real what they were dealing with. But I felt it took center stage and again, that I didn't like. No balance.<br /><i>Qhuinn</i> pushed some hard buttons here. I knew he would. I expected it. But dang. Even I got a few black eyes from those verbal punches he was throwing at <i>Layla &amp; Blay</i><br />He threw the biggest dang tantrums of epic proportions. He really did. LOL!<br />But it worked out. So there's that ;)<br /><br /><i>
  <b>Wrath</b>
</i><br />*Sighs* He's my man. He really is. He held it down here. As always. It's very hard to hate on that. I love him &lt;3 But every time he gets a headache, I just want to punch people for him.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>The Bastards</b>
</i><br />I loved seeing these males in their elements. Being in their thoughts, seeing them co-existing with <i>Xcor</i> and the <i>Brothers.</i> They are no longer faceless beings with weird names to me. I see the potential here and I'm very excited to learn more about each of these guys individually. I think they're awesome. And seeing them exercise their own personal code of honor while remaining loyal to their leader was touching.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>Lassiter</b>
</i><br />I love him when he's a good mixture of the serious &amp; lighthearted. He's just more compelling that way for me. I truly hope that Ward continues to development him more and more in this manner. He broke my heart with some of the things that was revealed here, concerning him and his "Learning Curve" with his new role. I can't wait to see more.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>Vishous</b>
</i><br />WHY?!!! Just why? I'm truly not happy with this sad excuse for a drama plot. *Rolls eyes* And it had a nice long time on the stage in this book, too. Seriously Ward, either sh&amp;t or get off the pot with these two. (Vishous &amp; Jane)... I and the whole world that knows of this series, knows that you've never truly wanted these two together. It's obvious in the way these two have always been written. But why even take it here and now? Why? *shakes head*<br /><br /><i>
  <b>Throe</b>
</i><br /><b>OHMYGOODNESS!</b><br /> WTHeck kinda fresh hell has he gotten himself into? <br /><i>This</i> was some dark mess. *shudders*<br /><br /><i>
  <b>The Climactic Fight Scene</b>
</i><br />I really loved it. WOW. I thought it was great and I missed seeing this type of action in this series. Let's get back to awesome basics here. #LovinIt<br /><br /><i>
  <b>The Ending</b>
</i><br />Bottom line I liked it, in theory. But I didn't love it, on paper. It was just way too sweet and too soon, and just too much right now, for all that was still lacking before it got to that point.<br /><br />Overall, I was truly curious about what Ward was going to do with this book. I was hoping she got back to her awesome, poignant story telling here. I mean she had so many great things to work with. But sadly, it just wasn't what I had hoped. This was just an <i>"Okay"</i> chapter to this series for me. If you're committed to the BDB as many of us are, then yes, you still need to read it for yourself. Just be aware that your feels for this could go either way. Take you anywhere. You may find yourself stuck in this alternate universe like me, trying to figure out just what happened exactly &amp; why.. <i>OR</i> you may actually love it *Shrugs*<br /><br />~~I will always love this series simply for what it once was. What pulled me in and caused me to stay for so long. I will always have love &amp; <i>hate</i> for the many characters involved here. But the truth is, it's simply not the series that it once was for me. The writing has changed. And honestly, that's not a good thing. It's a sad thing. At least for me.~~<br /><br />Much Love, my fellow BDB Brothers' &amp; Sisters'</span>
  <a data-text-id="12940165418050402590" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1725345972" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1725345972" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1725345972?book_show_action=true">Aug 11, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pnr-vampires">pnr-vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1725345972" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18372072094789711716"><b>4.5 ‘All hail Layla’ stars!</b><br/><br/>This book was a real mixed bag for me. Book #15 in the <i>Black Dagger Brotherhood</i> series, the build up to this love story has been coming for a long time, and I couldn’t wait to get my hands on Xcor and Layla’s book. There were shocks and surprises, heartbreak, excitement, huge reveals and heart-pounding excitement. Things I loved, and things (people <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Qhuinn <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>) I hated, but it was a wild ride, and I could not put it down. <br/><br/>The main focus, of co</span>
  <span id="freeText18372072094789711716" style="display:none"><b>4.5 ‘All hail Layla’ stars!</b><br /><br />This book was a real mixed bag for me. Book #15 in the <i>Black Dagger Brotherhood</i> series, the build up to this love story has been coming for a long time, and I couldn’t wait to get my hands on Xcor and Layla’s book. There were shocks and surprises, heartbreak, excitement, huge reveals and heart-pounding excitement. Things I loved, and things (people <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Qhuinn <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>) I hated, but it was a wild ride, and I could not put it down. <br /><br />The main focus, of course, is the love story between Xcor and Layla. A secretive, forbidden romance between the quiet, shy and dignified Chosen, Layla and badass leader of the Band of Bastards and enemy of the Brotherhood, Xcor. Their love story has been slowly unfolding in the background of the last few books and now, the secret is out and OMG! I was expecting fireworks, but they came from a direction in wasn’t expecting in a way that shocked me to my core! The emotion, the intensity, it absolutely blew me away, and the fallout impacts everybody involved in ways they never could have imagined. <br /> <br />But it provides the perfect opportunity for Layla to absolutely shine. She is a one fierce female, and I absolutely LOVED seeing her come into her own in this book! Formerly a Chosen, her life was spent in service to the race’s creator, and for the last few books she has been finding her way in the real world. And now she’s a proud mama who has found the love of her life and she is strong and fiercely protective, and holy hell she blew me away! I cheered for her over and over as she stood up for herself and her loved ones, and I was so proud of her. She truly is the hero of this book, and I freaking loved it!<br /><br />And Xcor. Such a complex character who was initially presented one way and who has gradually changed as we’ve seen more and more of him. This book gives us his full backstory, which I loved, as it provides some great depth and insight into his character, and it gets you feeling for him from the very beginning. His relationship with Layla has developed beautifully, and it has changed him, and I loved getting to see the gentler side of him - the honourable, loyal, respectful male so deeply in love with his female, he is both hot and seriously swoony as he finally opens his heart fully to her, and their against-the-odds love story is truly beautiful. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“With all of my black and withered heart, I love you, my female.”</i>
</blockquote><br />It’s a gorgeous and heartfelt romance, but with the main couple already madly in love, there was lots of time left for secondary storylines, and there are plenty of them! All of the Brotherhood is impacted by Layla’s perceived ‘treason’, and I was fascinated watching them all react to the reveal of her secret, and to the developments with Xcor, but there’s a whole lot of other things unfolding in the <i>BDB</i> world, and I loved the different storylines and POVs.<br /><br />Qhuinn – As the father of Layla’s young is a big player in the story and just…. Wow. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ One of my favourites of the series has had a complete personality transplant and it was like seeing a stranger as he revealed himself to be the biggest douche EVER! OMG! Where has <i>my</i> Qhuinn gone? Who is this asshole of epic proportions? And where the hell does he get off acting the way he does? The way he treated Layla, and even little Lyric, broke my heart, and I have no idea how he justified behaving the way he did. His words and actions were so out of character, and pretty much unforgiveable, and I wanted to junk punch him so hard! I’m so disappointed, and in the end I thought his absolution came WAY too easy. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Blay - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[He got totally shafted in this one too. Qhuinn was a dick not just to Layla, but to his mate as well, and after all that these boys have been through, all that Blay has put up with, this is another drama that he doesn’t deserves. He deserves so much better! But he shows his huge heart in his ability to forgive, and I’m happy that it ended well for him because in the end I just want to see him happy!!!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Tohr – His POV was a surprise, but I really enjoyed checking in with him. His part of the story gives a different perspective on the Xcor/Layla thing. But… <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[his grieving seems to be going on and on, and though I feel for him and his loss, I feel bad for Autumn who loves him so much but still seems like second best. And what was with his blow-up with Layla? Again, it seemed really out of character for him to be so disrespectful to a female! But I guess it shows the emotional intensity of all that he’s going through. And it’s not like he reached Qhuinn levels of dickdom. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br /><br />Wrath – We don’t get his POV, but he totally rocks it in this book. The Leader of the race shows just why he is such, and I loved him, and Beth. So much awesome. <br /><br />Trez - Interesting developments there, but is it too soon? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[And again, will it be a situation where Therese seems like second best? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I’m curious how it all fits together and how it’s all going to play out.<br /><br />Lassiter – Perfection as always. No great surprise where his storyline is taking him, and I cannot wait to watch it all unfold. I love him.<br /><br />New bad guy – Again, not a surprise who, but the how is intriguing. Not what I was expecting, but I’m curious what’s going to happen there. <br /> <br />Vishous - OMG, V! One of my absolute favourite Brothers is hitting a wall. It’s not surprising, but my heart aches for him. I’m hoping this book is the lead in to another book for him and Jane. I can’t wait to see where their story is going to go.<br /><br />The storylines all tie in together really well, and the book builds up to an epic showdown which will change the course of the Brotherhood forever. But for me, the ending felt a bit rushed and I was surprised at how quickly and easily everything seem to be resolved. There was so much hatred and animosity going on for most of the book and then suddenly it’s all over and everybody is happy again. Hmmmmm… it just seemed a bit easy.<br /><br />But as always, there is lots happening - some of it good, some not so good, but I loved how emotional this book made me. I was completely invested in the story, I loved how riled up I got, and the sweet and swoony moments melted me, and I struggled to put it down. I remain desperate for more as always. <br /><br />4.5 stars. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="18372072094789711716" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1904247987" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer326237751577817462"><b>Layla and Xcor!!! Its about Damn Time!!!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406691186ra/10585178.gif' width='400' height='284' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Holy Freakin Psycho Drama cause Qhuinn done lost his Shit and his Damn Mind! The conflict and drama in this one was off the chain..Not sure if I could hate Qhuinn more.<br/><br/><br/>***Spoiler Alert*** Rant Alert***Spoiler Alert***<br/><br/><br/>***Qhuinn...ASSHOLE of the year...Father of the year (NOT) ...immature and selfish as ever...and finally showing it to those closest to him. No Fucks given and Never apologizes for his behavior. <br/><br/><blockquote>Qhuinn pointed the gun right ar her through the </blockquote></b></span>
  <span id="freeText326237751577817462" style="display:none"><b>Layla and Xcor!!! Its about Damn Time!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406691186ra/10585178.gif" width="400" height="284" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Holy Freakin Psycho Drama cause Qhuinn done lost his Shit and his Damn Mind! The conflict and drama in this one was off the chain..Not sure if I could hate Qhuinn more.<br><br><br>***Spoiler Alert*** Rant Alert***Spoiler Alert***<br><br><br>***Qhuinn...ASSHOLE of the year...Father of the year (NOT) ...immature and selfish as ever...and finally showing it to those closest to him. No Fucks given and Never apologizes for his behavior. <br><br><blockquote>Qhuinn pointed the gun right ar her through the hole he'd made. "Drop them. Or I drop you."</blockquote></b><br><br>After threatening to kill Layla while she is holding his children, He fires his gun in the room with his children because he is upset with Layla for putting his children's safety at risk. * Hypocrite* He then goes on to ignore his daughter because she looks like Layla? *Father of the year*. He only makes amends when Blay forces his hand and makes him apologize.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"And you are going to be lucky to come out of this alive-not that I give a damn whether you live of or die. The only thing I care about is that you never see those young again-"</blockquote>
</b><br><br>I doubted his sincerity when he apologized. He showed no personal growth or reflection. Thank goodness Blay played hard ball with Qhuinn and moved out of the house. Otherwise Qhuinn would still be washing Layla's scent off the children.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"Better for them not to be born at all then to have half of you in them."</blockquote>
</b> <br><br><br><br>***Layla and Xcor....couple I've been pining for, with a serious hotness potential.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"In the course of my life, I have learned that dreams are not what come true, 'Tis only the nightmares that find you in real life. I had no real hope for this."</blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1561737004ra/27739241.gif" width="400" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I'm in the minority because I have enjoyed Layla's growth from mindless Chosen Eros Virgin, to Woman in love with a traitor, to Lioness protecting her young, to Standing up to Tohr in a verbal fight that had him wanting to hit her! Go Team Xcor &amp; Layla. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1561737004i/27739242._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I also liked Xcor from the start and loved his back story...but we only got a few snippets instead of the quality backstory this character deserved. He's the perfect misunderstood- villain. He also proved to be more honorable than Qhuinn and Tohr.<br><br><br><br><b>***Trez and Selena...I can't even give a shit about these two right now. It's too soon. Better yet, just wright his story right the 1st time instead of coming back trying to do a re-do.</b><br><br>Obviously Selena's been re-incarnated as Treece, but to give her the same exact face with no sacrifice? When Darius was brought back as John Mathew, the balance /sacrifice was that he wouldn't be able to speak. Selena looks exactly the same with no deficits, and Trez will love her because it's all about the looks and beauty...not what's inside?<br><br><br><br><b>***Lassiter, aka, couch potato, gets a promotion...which is better than what he was doing before....Absolutley nothing!!!</b><br><br>I'm in the minority because I'm not a Lassiter fan. He annoys me and not in a good, funny way. I'm not intrigued with his animal print pants and boas. I could care less about his new position and don't understand how a deity can die or no longer exist?<br><br><br><br><b>***V and Jane...marrital issues yet again....Yawn!! This relationship is so cold and clinical that V has to convince himself that they are OK. </b><br><br>Yet he nearly dies and she doesn't cry or show any emotion or hug him? WTF? She just runs off to see her next patient. That's not my definition of OK. I couldn't perform surgery if my husband lay dying from battle injuries. Plus, do these two ever do anything together outside of work and not have sex?<br><br>The drama with V and Jane is unresolved and I hope it it wrapped up in the next book or soon because I am starting to not give two shits about them. They are soooo lackluster and boring lately!<br><br><br><br><b>***Tohr...whom I haven't liked since his return. I Hated his love story with Autumn, who's name might as well still be No One, cause he treats her like she is no one important. </b><br><br>He's still grieving and missing his first wife who only died 2 years ago. His lack of love for Autumn annoys and disgusts me. I think he is just using her and could care less about her. <br><br>He also discovers he has a brother and immediately goes from hating him to hugging him in a 24 span? <br><br><br><br><b>***The Blind King... </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407458558i/10725508._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="586" alt="Wrath" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He kicks Layla out of the house, but Qhuinn just destroyed the door to get to Layla, threatened to kill her and fired a gun in the room with two newborns and in a house with other children?? The wrong one got kicked out. I'm just glad Wrath was very loving and kind to Layla when he visited her at the safe house. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>But the King held her in return, patting her back. "Do me a favor?"..."Be careful with Xcor. Even if he doesn't kill you physically, he can still ruin you for life."<br>"He already has, my Lord. The damage, I fear, is already done."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>There is no punishment for Qhuinn's behavior after the shooting, or allowing Xcor to escape, and he never found out about his involvement in the attempt on Xcor's life.<br><br><br>He kicks Tohr out of the BDB...only to rescind that order the very next day. So again...no punishment!<br><br><br><br><b>***Happy Ending***</b><br><br>So I have no idea how to rate this. There were parts that were a 3 star and a few 5 star moments. Still over all a very enjoyable book. The happy ending was all crammed into the last 3 pages. Qhuinn went from wanting to kill Layla and Xcor to hugs and jokes like they were all BFFs. <br><br>And The Band of Bastards are invited to live in the King's home after that badass fight. Yes, they they all refused to bend the knee to Wrath, but apparently that was OK as long as they follow Xcor.</span>
  <a data-text-id="326237751577817462" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1725675900" />
    <a title="Jonetta" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4876540-jonetta"><img alt="Jonetta" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1329083158p2/4876540.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1725675900?book_show_action=true">Aug 11, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jonetta" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jonetta" href="/user/show/4876540-jonetta">Jonetta</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audio CD 9781524756420" href="/book/show/31410968-the-chosen">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4876540-jonetta?shelf=4000-books">4000-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4876540-jonetta?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4876540-jonetta?shelf=250-series-up-to-date">250-series-up-to-date</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4876540-jonetta?shelf=17000-in-2017">17000-in-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4876540-jonetta?shelf=publisher-review-request">publisher-review-request</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4876540-jonetta?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4876540-jonetta?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4876540-jonetta?shelf=audio-1000">audio-1000</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1725675900" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5348712164868033021">Wow. What a crazy, train wreck ride! What else would you expect from the Brotherhood?<br/><br/>I have to come clean and admit I've never been a Xcor fan and have hated Layla's duplicity about her relationship with him. Because these stories have a multitude of storylines, I wasn't concerned about these two characters being the major focus as I was counting on the others to hold my interest. Xcor launched into this series as a cruel and brutal man, no way was there any possibility he could redeem himself i</span>
  <span id="freeText5348712164868033021" style="display:none">Wow. What a crazy, train wreck ride! What else would you expect from the Brotherhood?<br /><br />I have to come clean and admit I've never been a Xcor fan and have hated Layla's duplicity about her relationship with him. Because these stories have a multitude of storylines, I wasn't concerned about these two characters being the major focus as I was counting on the others to hold my interest. Xcor launched into this series as a cruel and brutal man, no way was there any possibility he could redeem himself in my mind and it irritated me that Layla betrayed the Brotherhood by continuing to see him. *sigh* I caved. <br /><br />Layla's revelation was received explosively, much more than I ever anticipated and my imagination was pretty creative. It set off a series of events that unsettled the Brotherhood and beyond, which hooked me through the end. It changed my opinion of some of the other characters (yes, that means you, Qhuinn), no matter how this ended. <br /><br />There were quite a few controversial situations in this story, some many may take serious issue with and I refuse to rehash the details. I'm not sure how I feel about some of them but I was very much drawn into this book. The storytelling is superb, the pace breakneck, the drama...well, dramatic. The narrator, Jim Frangione, continues to nail the characters and the crazy dialogue. I'll never go back to reading these books!<br /><br />I enjoyed this book immensely, even while some of the characters' directions angered me or offended my sensibilities. But isn't that what a good story is supposed to do? I also consider it a miracle that Ward made me end up rooting for Xcor and I'm still unsettled about that. I'll be waiting in line for the next one. Love it or hate it, you will not be bored. <br /><br />(I received an ARC from the publisher in exchange for an honest review)</span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7807887107262107674">4.5 ★'s <br/><br/><b>"You have saved me, and the only thing greater than my love for you is my gratitude."</b><br/><br/>As is the new usual for the BDB books, this story deals with Xcor and Layla's relationship, however, that is only a very small part of the book and there are multiple threads involved.<br/><br/>And that was unfortunate because I really came to like Xcor, someone I didn't really care for since we met him. I just have to say that I love his softer side and his past will break your heart. That doesn't mean that I thi</span>
  <span id="freeText7807887107262107674" style="display:none">4.5 ★'s <br><br><b>"You have saved me, and the only thing greater than my love for you is my gratitude."</b><br><br>As is the new usual for the BDB books, this story deals with Xcor and Layla's relationship, however, that is only a very small part of the book and there are multiple threads involved.<br><br>And that was unfortunate because I really came to like Xcor, someone I didn't really care for since we met him. I just have to say that I love his softer side and his past will break your heart. That doesn't mean that I think everything about him is wonderful and that he won't do something to screw things up OR something from his past will come back to haunt him/them because I definitely think it will. <br><br>I'm also not a Layla hater and I was happy that she finally found someone. I really liked how she stood up for her kids and Xcor and she's one smart cookie. The parts between her and Lassiter were pretty funny as well!<br><br>The major players in their story are the ones dealing with Xcor and Layla so that includes Qhuinn and Blay, Wrath, V and Tohr. There are some understandable reactions and then there are some that are wwwaaaayyyyy over the top and I am SHOCKED to say the least. Qhuinn lets us down, lets Layla down, lets Wrath down and most importantly, lets Blay down. And what he tried to do to redeem himself, well, it just didn't work for me. <br><br>The other stories have to deal with Lassiter, Trez and Therese, Throe and V. Lassiter is a no brainer especially if you're aware of the new twist. I do love his crazy side but I was expecting more of it. Hopefully, we will get it in the next book. <br><br>Trez and Therese was unexpected for me. I figured it would be some time, aka never, before Trez met someone and I'm a bit ambivalent about the circumstances. But...we've only gotten the beginning of the story so I'll withhold judgment for now.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402768830ra/9984496.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Holy Hell...what is going on with Throe? It's like he took an extreme left turn into all things stranger than fiction. But to be fair, I quit reading the Angel series so I may have missed some things that would make this clearer and after hearing things from J.R.W.'s signing, things are a lot more understandable. Still, not looking forward to this crazy train. <br><br>And lastly, but most importantly for me is V....OMG! WTH?? I'm flabbergasted to say the least and while I'm not happy about Jane's outcome in their book, I like their relationship and I'm just dreading going down this road. (although bring on the mothereffin' angst!) <br><br>You will either love or hate this book depending on the couples and/or the events...I still can't get over Qhuinn. But I will say one thing...this book shocked me, weirded me out, frustrated the hell out me but it also make me laugh and it definitely made me cry...especially the last part!<br><br>Next up is Assail and Sola's book, <i>The Thief</i>, coming out next year (2018). We got small pieces of him in this book and it wasn't good so fingers crossed that it will get better because I really like those two. Also, looking forward to more of BoB and my angst lovin' bad boy, V!</span>

<div id="review_2188362457" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bev " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bev " href="/user/show/14930441-bev">Bev </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14930441-bev?shelf=bloody-loved-it">bloody-loved-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14930441-bev?shelf=anti-hero">anti-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14930441-bev?shelf=don-t-mess-with-my-hea">don-t-mess-with-my-hea</a>
          </div>
